Gold and Silver 87

The London gold price rose by half a penny today to 138 shillings and one and a half pence.

The London silver market is still stable. There were American purchases and Chinese sales. The spot price is 21 and 5625 pence, up one two five. The futures price is 21 and 4375 pence, up zero six two five.

The Bombay silver market rose yesterday and fell slightly today. The spot price is 59 rupees and 10 annas. The August futures are 59 rupees and 11 annas. The September futures are 59 rupees and 13 annas. All fell by one pound.

Exchange Rates 88

This morning in the London foreign exchange market, the European continent sold US dollars. The Anglo-American exchange rate opened at five yuan and eight and a half fen, one two five lower than yesterday's closing US-British exchange rate. The price at 11 o'clock was five yuan, eight and eight seven five fen, up three seven five from the opening. At noon, it rose another five six two five fen, and at the close it rose again by one eight seven five fen, to five yuan and nine and six two five fen.

The Franco-British rate was unchanged at the opening, remaining at 76 francs 34, and fell six pounds at the close to 76 francs 28.

This morning in the New York foreign exchange market, the British pound was strong. The Anglo-American exchange rate opened up by one pound at five yuan and nine and six two five fen. This price remained stable for a long time, but the latest price is five yuan and nine and a half fen, down one two five from the opening. One US dollar is equivalent to three shillings and eleven and zero nine four pence.

Cotton and Wheat 89

The New York cotton market opened down by thirteen pounds. Before noon, the fluctuations were subtle and uneven. The latest price is one dime, three fen and five one, up one pound from the opening. Some predict that it will continue to rise later.

The New York wheat market opened down by five pounds because the wheat production report can be regarded as favorable to the short side, and because the Liverpool wheat market is very weak. However, the market price recovered slightly later, up two pounds from the opening.

The Bombay cotton price also fell today. The white Baloch cotton for the April-May period fell three and a half rupees to 234 rupees 25. The market is loose because the bulls are closing out.

The Liverpool wheat market is down today. The October futures fell two and a half pence.

Securities 90

Before the New York stock market opened, the favorable factors for the market were: (1) the quantity of freight loaded on trains, which can now be seen as exciting; (2) the work in the steel industry area, which has now reached 38% of its capacity, an increase of 1% compared to the beginning of the week; (3) public sentiment that at current prices, or when prices slightly decrease, many securities are worth buying. The unfavorable factors for the market are: (1) a weakening trend in commodity prices; (2) uncertainty about the future of commerce. People in the market are now extremely eager for its development. When the stock market opened this morning, the price fluctuations were small and uneven, but there was buying in mining stocks. The price of U.S. Steel stock rose by three points. The U.S. dollar remains weak, but the speculative psychology is gradually cooling down. It is expected that there will be no major fluctuations in general prices for the time being. Deployment of Soviet Russian Troops in Outer Mongolia and the Far East 106

Increasing troops and building camps to clearly show their attitude

Conspiracy activities, secret struggles, and ingenuity

Harbin News: The war situation in the Far East has reached a critical point. Both Japan and Russia are in a state of heightened tension. In addition to increasing troops and building camps in their respective areas and actively engaging in construction equipment to clearly show their attitude, they are also mutually exposing military intelligence. It is truly a scene before the eve of a major war. According to reliable sources, the Soviet government has selected a site in Outer Mongolia to build a large-scale barracks, which is currently housing a mixed unit of cavalry, artillery, and machine gun units. The details of the Soviet troops stationed in Outer Mongolia and the deployment of forces in the Far East are summarized as follows:

Troop Strength in Outer Mongolia 107

First, 18,000 elite troops were dispatched, with 42 cannons, 7 anti-aircraft guns, 130 heavy machine guns, 240 light machine guns, 12 aircraft, and 18 armored vehicles. The commander-in-chief of the above troops is Soviet General Ivanov Diétoula. His subordinates include 63 officers. Several airfields are reportedly under construction.

Troop Strength Between Hailar and Manzhouli 108

The total number of Soviet Russian troops between Vladivostok and Manzhouli is 140,000, including 15,000 special international security troops, 45,000 border security troops, and additional reserve troops (number unknown).

Military Aircraft Base 109

The total number of Soviet Russian military aircraft is 412, distributed in Khabarovsk, Svobodny, Razdolnoye, Bolshekhekhtsirsky, Bolshoy Ussuriysky. Because they fly frequently, the number of aircraft in each location cannot be investigated.

Troop Deployment Situation 110

(1) In the area from Svobodny to Nikolayevsk, there are four infantry divisions and one cavalry division. A large number of troops and military supplies are currently being transported from Europe to strengthen this area. (2) In the Yima area, there is a troop including an unknown number of Chinese. (3) In the Khabarovsk area, there is the headquarters of the Far Eastern Red Banner Army, commanded by Blücher. (4) Near the Amur area, there are three infantry divisions. (5) In the lower eastern part of Labaure, in Norchinsk, the troop strength is unknown; in Borkiaker Moskovsky and Chita, there are three infantry divisions and one cavalry division. (6) The troop strength in Deraryama Kistky is unknown. (7) In the Zabaykalsk area, there are three divisions of Mongolian Revolutionary Army cavalry. In total, there are two infantry divisions (actual number unknown), 300 tanks, 12 armored trains, and 12 submarines near Vladivostok.

Military Roads and Railways 111

(1) In December 1933, the military road from the Valkiyayevka station on the Amur line to the Nikolayevsk station was completed. (2) In December 1933, the construction of the military road from Manzhouli to Xianbusi, 85 li, was completed. (3) The railway between the Siberian Berezovsk station and the Mongolian Urkulty is under construction. In addition, within 5,000 kilometers of the border, residents must obtain permission from the GPU (secret police) to move their residence to prevent people from escaping. (Northeast News Agency)

Reception of Malanyu and Custody of Qing Tombs 112

Only the withdrawal of Japanese troops is lacking

All preparations are ready

Tianjin Correspondence: The reception of Malanyu, through the consultations between Yin Rugeng and Shibayama, has recently been scheduled for implementation within the month. However, the reception date has not been agreed upon due to Yin Rugeng's illness. It is reported that when Malanyu is received, in addition to the establishment of a branch office of the Jiji Administrative Commissioner's Office, there will be no other new organizations. As for the custody of the Eastern Tombs, our side will establish a custody committee, with Yin Rugeng as the chairman, the director of the Malanyu Commissioner's Office branch office, the magistrate of Xinglong County, and a Qing Dynasty prince residing in Pingjin as standing committee members. Sixteen articles of rules of procedure have been established for custody. Lost sacrificial vessels will be retrieved by any means possible. For years, because the tombs were in the war zone, no one took care of them, resulting in the theft of trees within dozens of miles around. This spring, the puppet Jehol army stationed in the area colluded with treacherous local people and secretly cut down trees. Even small saplings were stolen and sold. Therefore, from Malanyu to the Eastern Tombs, only stumps remain, with not a single tree left. This time, the puppet side proposed conditions for our custody, requesting that the Eastern and Western Tombs be merged for custody, expanding the establishment of the custody committee, allocating a certain amount of funding, recruiting tomb-guarding security teams, having the commissioner stationed at both tombs year-round, and planting trees. Our side believes that the Western Tombs are in our territory and have always been well-maintained, so there is no need to mention them together with the Eastern Tombs. Because the Eastern Tombs are outside Malanyu, the reception of Malanyu will complete the administration of Xinglong County. Therefore, the tomb area must be received and kept together. Otherwise, we have not recognized the legitimacy of the puppet court in Guandong, so how can we take care of their tombs? The Eastern Tombs originally had 30 tomb-guarding soldiers, but their firearms were confiscated by the Japanese army after the war. This time, new guns will be issued after the reception, without recruiting any additional tomb-guarding teams to avoid excessive waste. Previously, the chairman of Hebei Province, Yu Xuezhong, told people that Malanyu is our land. Only after the Battle of the Great Wall did the Japanese army move in and place it under semi-military occupation. Our magistrate of Xinglong County has established administration locally, and all organizations are ready. Only because the Japanese army does not withdraw can the government not fully exercise its power. The Tanggu Truce stipulates that Japanese troops will withdraw from various places along the Great Wall within one year. Everything related to our side in the Truce has been fulfilled, but the Japanese side has not done one thing. Malanyu has no so-called reception. It originally belonged to our land, and we should have administrative organizations. Only the withdrawal of Japanese troops is lacking. The so-called reception now has a tendency to expand and publicize. We are determined to handle the custody of the Qing Tombs unconditionally. If it contains some conditions and is carried out with solemnity, we will definitely not do it, etc. (8th)

Amidst the Commuinist Bandit Offense in Fujian

Guangdong Border Strengthens Defense 113

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, the communist bandit disasters in Fujian Province have become increasingly urgent. Chiang Bo-cheng, the liaison commissioner of the Central Army stationed in Guangdong, received a telegram on the 4th from Jiang Dingwen, commander-in-chief of the Eastern Route Army, reporting on the bandit situation, roughly as follows: (1) Parts of the puppet 79th Army Corps and miscellaneous communist bandits, about 9,000 in total, led by Luo Binghui, are fleeing through Yong'an and Youxi, seemingly plotting to flee to western Fujian. (2) North of Longyan, a part of the puppet 14th Division and local communists, about 4,000 in total, are taking advantage of the situation to rob food and flee without a fixed location. Li Yannian is searching and suppressing them, and many bandits have been killed. (3) Because the puppet army corps suffered too many casualties, they have incorporated the local Young Pioneers, model battalions, Red Guards, etc., into the various army corps. (4) The puppet 135th Army Corps, after being defeated by our Tang Column in the area south of Baishui, is now entrenched in the area north of Shicheng. In this battle, more than 700 bandits, including the regiment commander, were killed, and more than 100 guns were captured. (Omitted below) Jiang Dingwen, Jiang Yin, and others, in addition to reporting the bandit situation by telegram, also requested the Guangdong authorities to send troops to Fujian to assist in the suppression. (August 7th)

Anhui Province Relieves People's Food Shortages 114

Disaster Relief Association Asks the Provincial Government to Borrow Money

Relend to Various Counties to Hold Down Grain Prices

Anqing Correspondence: The Anhui Provincial Disaster Relief Association believes that this year's natural disasters are prevalent, and drought is rampant. Under this serious situation, adjusting the people's food supply is the only way to relieve the emergency at present. Therefore, it held a temporary meeting the other day. At the meeting, Standing Committee Member Fang Xiaoyuan proposed that since the drought has already formed and rice prices are rising, such as in Wangjiang and Tongcheng counties, disturbances have already occurred. Now, for the sake of emergency treatment, the provincial government should implement the borrowing of large amounts of money from the banking sector and relend it to various counties to hold down grain prices, in order to save the people's food supply and maintain public order. It was resolved and passed, but this borrowing method should be the responsibility of each borrowing county to repay on time. However, the interest and depreciation losses are unavoidable. It is proposed that the interest be borne by the government and the depreciation losses be compensated by the counties themselves. The burden borne is also light, and the methods will be determined separately. A special letter has been sent to the provincial government for verification and handling. In addition, the association believes that the reports of drought from various counties, and the many telegrams requesting investigation, have reached dozens of counties. It is urgent to select appropriate personnel for investigation. In addition to using the savings from the association's temporary expenses, the insufficient amount has been telegraphed to the provincial government, ordering the Finance Department to allocate 2,000 yuan for subsidies. (9th)

Hubei Province Implements Work Relief 115

Construction to Begin First in 20 Counties such as Wuchang

Counties Set Up Offices to Substitute Work for Relief

Hankou Correspondence: Hubei Province's disaster relief measures are divided into three categories: emergency relief, work relief, and agricultural relief. Emergency relief is carried out in the most severely affected areas due to the lack of large funds. Agricultural relief is also unable to replant due to the lack of rain. Work relief is imminent. The provincial government recently formulated a seven-program plan, including purchasing water pumps, setting up siphons, opening up ponds and weirs, and dredging ditches. The estimated cost is 2.4 million yuan. The Disaster Relief and Famine Preparedness Committee has now drafted a construction outline based on this plan, which was passed and implemented at a meeting on the 10th. The main contents are: (1) The scope of work relief includes the following 20 counties for repairing ponds, weirs, and ditches: Wuchang, Echeng, Puqi, Huanggang, Huangpi, Guangji, Huangmei, Yunmeng, Xiaogan, Yingcheng, Hanyang, Xianning, Jiayu, Huang'an, Macheng, Xishui, Qichun, Yangxin, Daye, and Jingshan. Setting up siphon pipes will be tentatively set in ten places: Wutai Gate, Wufeng Gate, Sanyanqiao Gate, Baofeng Gate, Sigu Gate, Yangsiji, Kanjiage, and Zhanggong Embankment. Those installing pumping machine boats will be placed first in two lakes in the suburbs of Wuhan. (2) Agency Organization: Each work relief county will set up a work relief office, with one director, appointed by the county magistrate, one deputy director, appointed by the engineering team's chief engineer, and one auditing commissioner, jointly appointed by the financial team and the auditing team. Two clerks will handle all the affairs of the office under the orders of the director and deputy director. One secretary will be appointed, along with 10 to 20 supervisors, one surveyor, and one worker. At each place where a siphon pipe is set up, one craftsman and one assistant will be assigned. For the pumping machine boats, two craftsmen and two assistants will be assigned to each boat. (3) Disaster Worker Organization: Work relief workers will be standardized as strong men, with 25 people as a squad and ten squads as a regiment, totaling 250 people. Each squad will have a squad leader, and each regiment will have a regiment leader, both selected from among the honest and intelligent workers. (4) Allocation of Work Funds: A. Each county will excavate 20 new ponds, each requiring 9,000 cubic meters of earth. At 10 cents per cubic meter, 200 ponds will require 180,000 yuan. B. Each county needs to repair 20 existing ponds and weirs, each requiring about 1,500 cubic meters of earth. At 10 cents per cubic meter, 200 ponds will require 30,000 yuan. C. It is tentatively planned to excavate ditches with a length of 125 kilometers, with about 3,000 cubic meters of earth per kilometer. At 10 cents per cubic meter, 50,000 yuan will be required. D. 15-inch siphon pipes will be set up at each location, with four pipes per location, each costing about 2,000 yuan, so ten locations will require 80,000 yuan. E. Two 20-horsepower pumping machine boats, each costing 10,000 yuan, will require 20,000 yuan. The above five items total 360,000 yuan for work funds. This is the first step of the project planned with existing funds. As for installing pumping machines in various areas and building water diversion and drainage gates, dams, culverts, ditches, etc., implementation will be planned after work funds are available. (10th)

Drought Severity in the Eighth District of Songjiang 116

Each township in this county has suffered from drought for a long time. The rice seedlings are withered, and the disaster is fully apparent. Farmers are bailing water day and night, and they are all exhausted, with huge losses. Although there was rain at the beginning of this month, it stopped after a few minutes and then cleared up again. Now there has been no rain for another ten days. According to recent surveys, the drought in the eighth district, Shanyang, is the most severe in the entire county, with 30 or more towns and villages such as Qijiadun Township, with a disaster area of 4,500 mu. In order to relieve the suffering of the drought, the county's agricultural extension station purchased two bailing machines, which were purchased in Song a few days ago and will be transported to the disaster area for use in the near future. It also provided dozens of bags of buckwheat, mung beans, etc., and distributed them to farmers in five locations: Shanyang, Caojing, Jinshanwei, Jinshan Mouth, and Jiangzhuang, for planting. It is also learned that a large number of rice borers and locusts have been found in the rice fields of Yanduntou and other townships in Punan recently. Once they bite, the rice seedlings will wither immediately. If no measures are taken to eliminate them, the autumn harvest will be hopeless.

Taoist Disciples of the Jade Emperor Pavilion Found 117

Lu Zhonghe, the abbot and Taoist priest of the Jade Emperor Pavilion, has accepted five disciples, Da Ming, Da Zhen, Da Yuan, Da Ru, and Jiu Cheng, all of whom are underage. They disappeared from the temple on March 23rd while learning scriptures. After searching everywhere, there was no news. After reporting to the court to summon Lu Laotai, who was suspected, there was no evidence. It was ordered to be released on bail. Unexpectedly, on the 7th, a friend from Shanghai came to the temple to inform them that the lost disciples were hiding in a temple in Gujia Ting Temple, No. XX, Haichao Temple, Zhonghua Road, Shanghai. They were arrested on their behalf and sent to Song Yunyun. As expected, Da Ming, Da Zhen, and Jiu Cheng were sent back yesterday. Da Wu and Da Ru, it is said, have already returned home. It is said that the abductors were Yang Jianglin and others.

County Government Sends Personnel to Receive and Extradite Wanted Criminals 118

In the kidnapping case of Ni Bu Jin, the son of Ni Lai Sheng, from Shanzixing, Jinshanwei, the water patrol team arrested two kidnappers, Zhang A Zhao and Zhou A San. Because the area belonged to Jin County, they were sent to Jin for interrogation. The Ben Bao was logged. Afterwards, the team found out that Zhang A Zhao and others were the wanted criminals who shot and killed Zhang Zhipeng, the squad leader of the Jiangzhuang Police Team. They should be brought to justice to comfort the soul of the hero. The county government has prepared a document and sent Shen Shousheng, captain of Water Patrol Team No. 1, to Jinshan County to receive and extradite them.

Wuxi Rice Industry Automatically Limits Rice Prices 119

The county government of this county previously received a provincial order to limit rice prices. After submitting it to the administrative affairs meeting for discussion, the county sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce, which in turn sent a letter to the rice bean industry association, urging it to earnestly guide them. After receiving the letter from the Chamber of Commerce, the association submitted it to the 46th executive and supervisory committee meeting for discussion. It was agreed that this year's weather is arid, and the river channels are shallow, hindering transportation. The source of supply is scarce, and the purchases of various gangs are more concentrated. As a result, public sentiment is rising, and rice prices are gradually rising, with no nature of manipulation. Fortunately, last year's harvest was abundant, and warehouse stocks are still thick, which can be used for emergencies. Moreover, the new early indica rice in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has already entered the market. If the river water can rise slightly, it can still come in a steady stream. Shanghai has imported foreign rice, which will be imported into the interior in the future to regulate rice prices and maintain balance. It is not expected to have odd results. At present, the Shanghai market has a fixed case that white japonica rice should not exceed 13 yuan. Therefore, we should also respect the official care for the people's food and decide to automatically limit the white japonica rice to no more than 12 yuan per stone. A letter was sent back to the Chamber of Commerce, and yesterday it was transferred back to the county government for record.

River Dredging Dispute Causes Strike in the Entire Town 120

The Nan Yan Township Ganlu Town in the eighth district has a river that is silted up. Coupled with this year's arid weather, the river water is even shallower. Therefore, Zhang Zhiduan, the town chief of the town, initiated a meeting of all the residents of Yejijian to discuss and find ways to open the river. Ren Gencai from Hongdeji undertook the river dredging project. At that time, a total of 2,400 cubic meters of earth were measured, and it was stated that the wages per cubic meter of earth were 7 cents. By the other day, all the work was completed, and the wages had been paid in full. Unexpectedly, when the foreman Ren Gencai remeasured it, there were suddenly 6,800 cubic meters of earth. After deducting the previously paid amount, more than 3,000 yuan were still required. Town Chief Zhang argued that the difference was too great. However, the foreman relied on the crowd and acted barbarously. Yesterday morning, he led hundreds of workers, each holding wooden sticks, iron hoes, and other weapons, to disturb the town, intending to use force. At that time, the situation was serious, and the residents were panicked. All the shops in the town were on strike. Later, Town Chief Zhang reported the matter to the district branch and the public security branch, which sent police to the town to suppress it. By about 12 o'clock, the shops gradually reopened. On the one hand, Gao Shichun, the patrol officer of the branch, contacted the workers' representatives, but no agreement had been reached by the evening, and they were still insisting on their demands.

Long-Distance Bus Price Reduction Dispute 121

The Xicheng long-distance bus reduced its prices yesterday (the 11th). Wuxi to Jiangyin is 5 cents per person, Qingyang 4 cents, Tangtouqiao 3 cents, and Yanqiao 2 cents. Jiangyin to Qingyang is 3 cents. The fares are the same in both directions. Yesterday was the date of implementation. The business car owners, upon hearing this, believed that if it was implemented, their business would inevitably decrease. In order to maintain their livelihood, they stopped all the drivers. Unexpectedly, this aroused the drivers' resentment. Yesterday morning, dozens of them gathered and went to the county party headquarters to petition for relief. The county party headquarters agreed to convene the county government, the construction bureau, and others to discuss solutions. On the one hand, they notified the long-distance bus company to postpone the price reduction, but they were unable to comply. The drivers were very angry and drove the empty cars to solicit business in the middle of the road, creating a tense situation. The police arrived to maintain order. The matter had not been resolved by the afternoon.

Sixth District Discovers Large Swarms of Locusts 122

In the Sifang Bridge Houtangwan area, about four li northwest of Zhangjing Bridge in the Sixth District, large swarms of locusts were discovered at approximately 6:00 AM yesterday (the 11th). They stretched for about half a li. However, they have not yet developed wings. Currently, they are in the vicinity of major cemeteries, and the leaves on the graves have been completely devoured. Upon hearing the news, local villagers in the area were extremely alarmed. Swayed by superstition, they gathered hundreds of men and women to set up an altar and chant scriptures, hoping the locusts would go elsewhere. The loss to the crops in the fields is still slight, it is said.

Changzhou Public Security Bureau Uncovers a Narcotics Ring 123

On the 10th, the Wuyi County Public Security Bureau, based on a report from He Gengling, a patrol officer of the 7th Direct Jurisdiction Sub-station of Hutang Bridge, apprehended Zhao Shijun, a suspect involved in selling narcotic pills, along with sealed bags of the pills. Section Chief Wang Chongxian conducted a preliminary interrogation and traced the source of the pills. Zhao Shijun confessed that he purchased the pills from Yang Chuan'er at No. 3 at the base of the west city wall. Yang also entrusted him to sell them in the surrounding villages. Based on this information, Section Chief Wang believed that Yang Chuan'er's manufacturing and selling of narcotics could not be easily dismissed. He reported this to Bureau Chief Xu Baoguang, who ordered several officers to accompany Zhao Shijun to the address for investigation and arrest. A large number of pill-making tools and raw materials for narcotics were found in Yang's residence, and the principal offender, Yang Chuan'er, along with his mistress Zhu Qian, the homeowner Yang Zhanlan, and suspects Zhang Wenbi and Li Mubai, were apprehended. After a preliminary interrogation at the bureau, they were handed over to the county for further questioning on the 11th.

Seamen Police Officer Causes Trouble Through Horseplay 124

In Chang Le Town, Third District, police officer Wu Haoran of the Second Public Security Sub-bureau, at approximately 4:00 PM yesterday (the 9th), was playfully teasing A'bao, the eleven-year-old son of merchant Huang Wenzhi, inside the bureau. Wu aimed a toy gun at A'bao as if to shoot him. Unexpectedly, there was still a bullet in the gun that had not been removed. The trigger was accidentally pulled, and with a "bang," the bullet struck A'bao in the lower abdomen. He immediately collapsed and died from profuse bleeding. Police officer Wu was placed under guard by Sub-bureau Chief Li Dequan and was transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for questioning this morning (the 10th).

Ministry of Military Affairs Dispatches Personnel to Investigate Military Assets 125

The Su Lang garrison of the Reclamation Special District used to be approved by Zhang Jian to be transferred to the Tonghai Reclamation Company. Two years ago, Yu Bujiud and others accused the company of illegal occupation and filed a complaint with the Ministry of Military Affairs. As a result, the ministry ordered the company to pay for the land. However, this case has many complications and remains unresolved. Yesterday (the 9th), the Ministry of War specifically dispatched Hu Qin, the director of the First Military Assets Investigation Team, to Haimen to investigate, and ordered the county government to assist in the matter.

Nantung Governing the Yangtze River Establishes County Delegates 126

The Governing the Yangtze River Committee, composed of ten counties along the coast, has had its delegates appointed by the Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee. They are: Chen Baochu of Nantong, Wang Dankui of Chongming, Gu Haojia of Jiangyin, Zhu Kai Chou of Taicang, Zhang Bochu of Chuansha, Yu Mingde of Rugao, Tan Juenong of Haimen, Zhu Zongdao of Changshu, Zhao Zhengping of Baoshan, and Gu Yueseng of Qidong. The committee's headquarters will be located in Nantong. The first general meeting, originally scheduled for mid-September, has been rescheduled to be held in Zhenjiang due to transportation issues.

Yangzhou Baoguang Temple Hill Uncovers a Red Pill Manufacturing Ring 127

Acting on a confidential report, the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau discovered that Chu Ping, the abbot of Baoguang Temple in Nanchenglimen, secretly established a ring to privately manufacture and sell red pills, and was also involved in opium consumption. Early in the morning on the 10th, the bureau dispatched Team Leader Lang Huizhang, along with armed police officers, to the specified location. In a secret room, they found a small rainbow of raw materials for red pills, approximately several dozen kilograms, eight small packets of morphine, heroin, and other narcotics, as well as opium pipes and trays. They also apprehended important suspects Gao Buyuan and You Ganchen, as well as six monks and young novices from the temple: De Feng, Jiang Zhaofu, Jia Jiren, Jia Xiangjun, and Sun Jincai, all of whom were taken to the bureau. The main suspect, Chu Ping, took the opportunity to escape and hide in the home of a Zhang family in Nanmen. The bureau discovered this and sent officers to arrest him. During interrogation, he confessed to the sales. Furthermore, at the home of Wang Dong, near the temple, sixty packets of red pills, totaling over six thousand pills, were found. According to Dong, Chu Ping had stored them there. The Public Security Bureau has reported this to the County Government for review.

Severe Drought in Lin'an County 128

Since the beginning of summer, the county has not received a drop of rain, and the drought has lasted for more than two months. Recently, there have been occasional drizzles, but they stop as soon as they start, providing little benefit. Of the four districts in the county, it is reported that only about six-tenths of the seedlings have been planted, and they appear withered and stunted, barely reaching a foot in height. The vast fields of parched seedlings could easily be set ablaze. The unplanted rice paddies are cracked and fissured, the soil as hard as brick. Moreover, the major streams have dried up, and the deep wells are depleted. Residents near the mountains must travel three to five li to find spring water for drinking. The demand for water is even greater in the city, where people form lines for three to four hours, vying for water, with latecomers often finding none. The water is sometimes extremely dirty and foul-smelling, but it is better than nothing. Even household ponds and small wells have been almost completely drained. As a result, the people are in a state of anxiety and panic. The farmers, gaunt and emaciated, spend their days gazing at the sky, hoping for rain, their faces full of despair, leaving one wanting to cry. Although there was a slight drizzle a few days ago, it was of no help. However, water is seeping into the streams and wells, making the water cleaner to drink. As for the fields, the small amount of water is not even enough to moisten the soil. According to experienced farmers, if there is heavy rain within the next three to five days, there may be a thirty to forty percent chance of saving the crops; otherwise, this year's autumn harvest is doomed.

Robbers Kill Farmer in Huzhou 129

In the Caojia Hui area, north of the city, lived a farmer named Ling Changsheng, who enjoyed a modest prosperity, making him a target for bandits. He had been robbed five or six times in the past three years. Unexpectedly, at approximately 1:00 AM on the 8th of this month, more than ten bandits, each armed with guns, broke down the door and entered, searching at will. They stole more than thirty articles of clothing and over one hundred yuan in cash. When Ling Changsheng saw the bandits enter, he immediately climbed onto the roof and beat a gong, but he was shot by the bandits, the bullet piercing his abdomen. He fell from the roof and died instantly. Afterward, Ling's son, A Fa, came to Huzhou to report the incident to the court. After the court report, yesterday at around 10:00 AM, officials were dispatched to the village to conduct an investigation.

International Situation 137

Reporters then asked Yan about the recent situation between Japan and Russia. He said that it is difficult to predict the current situation between Japan and Russia. Since the Disarmament Conference failed to produce results, all countries are doing their best to expand their military preparations. No Discussion of Diplomacy 138

The United States Increases the Price of Silver

Hinders Our Foreign Trade 145

He Bingxian and Jin Guoshi Share the Same View

According to the Shenshi News Agency, after the United States implemented its silver policy, the price of silver has been rising steadily, and its impact on China's financial and industrial sectors is becoming increasingly serious. A Shenshi News Agency reporter visited He Bingxian, the director of the International Trade Bureau, and Jin Guobao, a banker, and asked for their opinions. Both agreed that China's export trade would inevitably suffer a major blow. Details are as follows:

He Bingxian Talks About the Impact on Trade 146

According to He Bingxian, the director of the International Trade Bureau, the recent increase in the price of silver in the United States has led to a large outflow of silver from China. In theory, a large outflow of silver will inevitably lead to financial chaos and a decline in paper money, which will have a significant impact on the monetary system. However, judging from the current situation, it is difficult to predict whether there will be such a danger in the future, as the increase in the price of silver in the United States has not yet significantly affected China. However, the increase in the price of silver will definitely have a major adverse effect on China's foreign trade, which can be determined. When the price of silver was not increased, China bought foreign goods with silver at a very high price, and foreigners bought Chinese goods with gold at a very low value. Under this situation, China's exports of goods were more than imports of foreign goods, which could be offset to a considerable extent. Now that the price of silver has increased, because China uses high-priced silver,

China's Grass Cloth Should be at a Minimum

Have the Same Tax Rate as Japanese Cotton Cloth 147

The Grass Cloth Guild Submits a Request

Premier Wang Negotiates with Japan

Weng Qifan, chairman of the Sichuan Grass Cloth Industry Association in Shanghai, submitted a document to Premier Wang stating that grass cloth sold to Korea and Japan is subject to high taxes. He presented his views in order to negotiate and achieve the principle of reciprocity. The association previously read the Customs' announcement of the tax exemption order for grass cloth, which shows that the court loves domestic goods, encourages exports, and has good policies and benevolence. They did not dare not praise it. After reading the July 14th report, Minister Kong talked about the government revising the import tariff, specifically hiring experts to study it. Although the tariff on Japanese goods was reduced, the reason was for the sake of reciprocity. For example, Japan levies high taxes on grass cloth, and without this, it would not be possible to demand a reduction. This is because the court is seeking to establish a position for domestic goods and promote overseas trade, not hesitating to exchange huge benefits, especially for grass cloth. All hundreds of thousands of businessmen in the grass cloth industry are deeply grateful. After checking, China's new import tariff has already been promulgated and implemented, but Japan has not reduced its tax on Chinese grass cloth, and the court has not clearly expressed it, meaning that it is still under negotiation. The association's grass cloth has been sold in Korea for the longest time. In the past, Japan levied taxes in four grades: 18 yuan per 100 jin for top rough cloth, 21 yuan for rough cloth, 32 yuan for slightly fine cloth, and 40 yuan for fine cloth. Later, seeing the development of the grass cloth sales market, it implemented a tax increase in the 16th year of the Republic of China: 22 yuan per 100 jin for top rough cloth, 34 yuan for rough cloth, 52 yuan for slightly fine cloth, and 72 yuan for fine cloth. The industry suffered a lot from the high tax, and the losses were not small. Then came the Korean riots, and the direct and indirect losses were even greater. The industry was almost paralyzed. In the year before last, the country used the excuse that fine cloth was 19 inches wide and increased the tax by 35%. Last summer, the rough cloth was also increased by 35%. Now, the tax paid per 100 jin of top rough cloth is 32 yuan and 40 cents, 45 yuan and 90 cents for rough cloth, 70 yuan and 2 cents for slightly fine cloth, and 97 yuan and 20 cents for fine cloth, which is almost 100% of the value, making it the most burdensome tax in the world. In the past, during the peak sales era, Sichuan grass cloth reached 2 million yuan, and Jiangxi grass cloth doubled it. In recent years, the total grass cloth from Jiangxi and Sichuan provinces is less than 1 million yuan. Once the industry is unable to bear the losses, it will stop operating there. Now, fortunately, the court is considering the difficulties of merchants, revising the reciprocal trade agreement, and focusing on grass cloth tax reduction, which may provide a glimmer of hope. After checking, China has reduced taxes on many Japanese imports. China only sells one type of product in Korea, which is grass cloth. At a minimum, it must follow the same tax rate as the country's cotton cloth in order to be consistent with the principle of reciprocity. Otherwise, reciprocity is in name only, and burdensome taxation is in reality. Economic aggression is the common practice. The court has deep thoughts and far-reaching plans, and its diplomatic negotiations have a plan in mind, which does not need to be disturbed by the association's knowledge. However, the association's business of grass cloth is of great concern, and it cannot help but speak out. It offers its humble advice, and the court is invited to adopt it. The ability of grass cloth to develop in overseas trade in the future is based on this negotiation. Please strive for public reason and be fearless, and only after achieving the goal of reciprocity will it be over. If there is something appropriate, please follow the instructions. Respectfully submitted to President Wang of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, Chairman Weng Qifan of the Sichuan Grass Cloth Industry Association in Shanghai.

the foreign goods purchased at low prices will inevitably increase, and the foreigners who buy my valuable domestic goods with low-priced gold will inevitably decrease. Therefore, China's foreign trade has a great relationship with the US silver price increase policy.

Jin Guobao Expresses Pessimism 148

According to economic expert Jin Guobao, opinions among Chinese economists are divided on the advantages and disadvantages of increasing the price of silver for China. However, based on his personal observations, he feels that increasing the price of silver is actually detrimental to China. The United States has adopted an expansionary policy, buying up silver from various countries around the world. Based on the current price of silver, the New York market is already higher than China. China's silver reserves will inevitably flow out, resulting in a contraction of China's currency supply. At the same time, it will also affect the decline in China's prices. With this cycle, China's rural economy will inevitably be greatly disrupted. In addition, China's emerging industrial products will inevitably be affected by the silver price increase, making them unable to be exported, while foreign goods can continue to flow in. In this situation, the amount of import surplus will definitely increase, and the number of silver outflows will also increase accordingly. Therefore, if the US silver policy continues to be implemented, China's financial and industrial markets will definitely feel great anxiety.

In This City

Property Tax Slightly Increased 149

Collected at 12 Percent of the Rent

Decision to Implement from the Winter of This Year

According to a responsible person from the city's Finance Bureau, Shanghai is a world-famous city and must have considerable basic municipal facilities. In recent years, efforts have been made to implement the Greater Shanghai Plan, and efforts should be made to realize it. However, striving to realize it, construction is the priority. As construction projects increase day by day, the costs and maintenance costs are also increasing day by day. According to the habits of civilized society, this cost should be borne separately by the citizens. This is the right and obligation that citizens should enjoy, and the principle is very clear and simple. It is found that the property tax is a major source of income for the city. The property tax rate for residents has only been collected at 10 percent. Therefore, it is necessary to increase it appropriately. After being approved by the central government, the city's property tax for residents will be changed to 12 percent of the rent, which will still be borne half by the owner and half by the tenant. The increased amount of tax will only be used to inject funds into the above-mentioned municipal facilities. However, the increased tax rate is also very fair. The patrol tax collected in the special zone is 13 percent in the French Concession and 14 percent in the Public Concession. 12 percent for road sections built beyond the boundary are all borne entirely by the tenant. In terms of the tenant's burden, the city is still several times away from the special zone. Before the 18th year of the Republic of China, during the era of collecting general taxes, the property tax rate for residents was 6 percent, which was completely paid by the tenant. Now, 12 percent is collected, and the landlord and tenant each pay half, so the tenant only pays 6 percent. This new tax rate was originally approved from this year (ie July).

Decided to Form a Subcommittee to Study 152

The discussion then began. There was unanimous agreement on the principle of the law. Various Banks All Agree to the Revision 153

The deadline was last night. Replies have been received from more than 40 banks, including Coal Industry, Dazhong, and Jianghai, all of which unanimously agreed. The association decided to start today next week, immediately make a formal presentation and send it to various non-member banks for stamping, and then submit it to the Yuan Ministry to request revision.

The General Federation of Industry Telegraphs the Guangdong Province

Cancel Special Tax on Domestic Goods 158

The Number of Foreign Factories Can Be Counted on Fingers

Imposing a General Tax Is No Different from a Likin

The Chinese General Federation of Industry yesterday telegraphed Guangdong Province, requesting the cancellation of the special tax on domestic goods entering the province. The original telegram stated: "Southwest Political Committee, Guangdong Provincial Government, greetings. Recently, it has been heard that the industrial and commercial sectors of your province are using the excuse that Shanghai factories have a large number of foreign investments and are dumping goods in Guangdong to vigorously advocate that the authorities implement taxation to protect the province's industry. It is also heard that local chambers of commerce have been convened to discuss and decide to establish a bureau to collect special taxes on imported goods and goods entering the province from other provinces. It is found that Shanghai is a trading port of our country, and it is inevitable that foreign merchants will set up factories in Shanghai. According to what our association knows, only the textile and cigarette industries in Shanghai have a slight advantage. Under the competition and struggle of domestic goods in other industries, they have gradually declined, and their numbers are already less than one-twentieth of domestic factories. Whether it is Chinese or Western, not only the competent authorities know in detail, but also the people of the whole country know clearly. However, the industrial and commercial sectors of your province do not pay attention and take the opportunity to demand an increase in the import tax from other provinces. After a little investigation of this proposal, it is known that it is a special tax in name, but a likin in reality. Once implemented, domestic goods will inevitably be destroyed. Since our country has had tariff autonomy, all domestically produced machine-made foreign-style goods are mostly only subject to transit taxes, and no other taxes are levied. Now, your province has added a special tax to prevent the dumping of goods from various provinces and protect the province's industry and commerce, which is a general term that does not distinguish between Chinese and foreign. Therefore, our association believes that this measure can only be applied to foreign goods, and domestic goods should not be treated the same way. Otherwise, the industrial products of all ports in the country will inevitably be unable to be sold in Guangdong Province due to heavy taxes, which will affect the industry, not just Shanghai. Moreover, if your province takes the lead, other provinces will inevitably follow suit, rejecting each other, and few will not perish together. Our association is the general hub of national industry and bears the mission of leading and safeguarding domestic industry. We dare to represent the national industry and telegraph to your association to cancel the proposal to collect special taxes on domestic goods, in order to save domestic factories from the brink of danger. I am extremely grateful. Chinese General Federation of Industry."

Yellow Car Company

Drivers on Strike Yesterday 160

The Above Put Forward Four Demands

Dagon Gazette: The Yellow Car Company, a Chinese-owned business, has its main station at 534 Avenue Dubail in the French Concession, and has branch stations at seven locations, including Avenue de la Gare, Suzhou Road, Yuyuan Road, the Bund, Route Pichon, Avenue Edward VII, and Route Frelupt. It has a total of 56 cars and employs 133 regular and deputy drivers. Recently, due to dissatisfaction with the company's treatment, they suddenly announced a joint strike at 1 a.m. yesterday and went to the Car Drivers' Union on Mingguo Road for a meeting to put forward their demands and request assistance from party and government agencies. Therefore, the company's business has been completely suspended since yesterday morning.

Reasons for the Labor Dispute 161

According to the statement of all the drivers of the Yellow Car Company, the reasons for the labor dispute are as follows: (1) In January of this year, worker Zhou Yintai knocked down a pedestrian on Zhabei South Bridge. After the company investigated the matter, it was found that the fault belonged to the pedestrian. All compensation for damages had already been admitted and paid by the company itself, but it went back on its word afterwards and still made Zhou Yintai bear the responsibility himself, which was unfair. Also, worker Wang Langen damaged a vehicle on Fuxu Road last month. The damaged part was old, but the company ordered compensation for the new value, which was also unfair. (2) Workers Chi Miaogen, Zhou Huicheng, and Yan Asan had already handed over the passenger signature slips to the relevant staff. Later, the relevant staff carelessly lost the signature slips. The company ordered the above three people to compensate for the fares listed on the signature slips. (3) The company's current business is more prosperous than before, with monthly revenue of over 20,000 yuan, but the workers' wages have fallen as before, making it difficult to live. (4) There is no rest time for day and night service, and the workers are mentally exhausted and prone to accidents. (5) Workers Lu Xincai, Chen Jinshi, Ren Changshan, and others were fired by the company for trivial matters. (6) The company's newly promulgated Article 5, Article 18, and Article 22 of the Driver Service Regulations are too oppressive to the workers. (7) Workers' jobs are too insecure. (8) Workers' lives are too harsh.

Four Demands 162

After all the workers went on strike, they put forward the following four demands: (1) The company should immediately return the compensation paid by Chi Miaogen for the fares listed on the lost signature slips. Zhou Huicheng and Yan Asan should be exempted from the responsibility of paying the same compensation. (2) Reinstate Lu Xincai, Chen Jinshi, Ren Changshan, and other three workers. (3) Revise the newly promulgated Driver Service Regulations. (4) Improve all treatment and sign treatment conditions.

Company Statement 163

A Dagon Gazette reporter went to the company's main station on Avenue Dubail yesterday afternoon to interview Manager Lin Zhongming, who said that the truth of the workers' sudden strike was completely unclear. Since the strike, no representatives have been sent to contact the company or put forward any demands. Now that the labor dispute has occurred, we can only wait for the party and government agencies to deal with it according to law. However, we hope that the workers will not go to extremes for the sake of labor-management cooperation. The company has prepared a memorial to request the municipal party department and the Social Affairs Bureau to handle it.

Party Department Investigation 164

Upon receiving the report, the Municipal Party Department attached great importance to the strike at the Yellow Car Company because it concerned local transportation. The investigation section immediately sent a cadre, Yu Yaoqiu, to the company and the workers to investigate the truth and report it for approval. It was also decided that the Civil Affairs Section of the Party Department would join the Social Affairs Bureau tomorrow to summon both parties to mediate according to law, so as to avoid prolonged disputes and losses to both parties.

Rickshaw Dispute Ends 165

All Vehicles Released, Rickshaw Drivers Operate as Usual

Court Adjourns Hearing Yesterday, Continuing Interrogation at a Later Date

The New News Agency reports that some rickshaw drivers in the Public Concession were dissatisfied with the solution reached by the Car Committee and the car dealers, which caused disturbances on the streets on the 9th and 10th of the month. After the police arrested them strictly, the situation returned to normal yesterday. The details are as follows:

Return to Normal 166

On the 9th and 10th, some rickshaw drivers, using the excuse that the Municipal Council and the car dealers had compromised on revising the new regulations, oppressed the rickshaw drivers, so they blocked rickshaws on the streets and deflated the tires, carrying out sabotage. The Municipal Council believed that this behavior of the rickshaw drivers not only hindered traffic, but also incited strikes and disrupted public order, so it ordered the police stations to strictly arrest them and arrested the main actors, Zheng Fazhu, Zhu Fengxiang, Cang Gongwen, and others one after another. The rickshaw drivers who went to the Car Committee to petition on the 9th held a temporary emergency meeting on Xiaoshadu Road on the evening of the 10th and sent 40 representatives to various roads to persuade them to stop the damage. Therefore, all the vehicles of the car owners were released as usual yesterday, and the rickshaw drivers also operated as usual with peace of mind.

Court Hearing 167

The police authorities learned that the leaders of this incident were Jiangbei natives Zheng Fazhu and others, so the Chinese and Western detectives of the Political Department went to arrest the representatives of the association, Zheng Fazhu, Zhu Fengxiang, Cang Gongwen, Cang Gongsen, and Xing Hongxi, and detained them in the Putuo Road police station. They were sent to the Criminal Division 2 of the First Special Court yesterday morning. The lawyer representing the police station rose and described the case in detail, saying that the police station is currently prosecuting Zheng Fazhu, Zhu Fengxiang, and Cang Gongwen for the crime of obstructing freedom under Articles 318 and 319 of the Criminal Law, but in the future, it may be necessary to add the crime of damage under Article 382 of the Criminal Law. The remaining Cang and Xing are not prosecuted for the time being, and they are requested to be detained. From the previous two days, a strike broke out among rickshaw drivers in the Public Concession, and they blocked rickshaws along the way, removing screws and deflating tires, making them unable to drive. After detailed investigation by the police station, it was learned that the five defendants in this case were the backbone of the initiators. They reported to the court and obtained arrest warrants at 11:30 last night to arrest the five people. Because the Municipal Council, according to the report of Gu Songmao, chairman of the Car Dealers Association, said that the rickshaws released in the past three days could not collect their rent, or the vehicles were destroyed, and they could not operate. Please find a way to protect them. While the police station was investigating, the five defendants served as representatives of 300 rickshaw drivers to petition the Political Department of the Municipal Council, demanding rent reduction. They thought the result was satisfactory and left, but soon the defendants held white flags and rioted along the way, deflating the tires and destroying the vehicles. Then they rushed to the wasteland on Rue Robert and gathered to hold a meeting, shouting slogans to overthrow the car owners, so that the rickshaw drivers would not pay rent and the car owners would not be able to operate. Therefore, the police station arrested Zheng and others. A ledger and leaflets were seized from Zhu Fengxiang's side. The ledger had the words "pay three corners" on it. According to the police station's speculation, rickshaw drivers who joined the strike and took charge of deflating tires were given three corners of foreign money every day. As for the leaflets, there were more than 20 initiators, and all five defendants were listed on them, specializing in sabotage. However, the content of this case is complicated, and the police station has not yet investigated it in detail, and requested permission to adjourn the hearing. The lawyer representing the Car Dealers Association stated that about 700 or 800 vehicles have been destroyed in recent days, with losses exceeding 10,000, so they filed a private prosecution. They agreed to the postponement of the hearing. When asked, the defendant Zheng Fazhu confessed that he runs a rickshaw shop with 20 rickshaws, and believes that he is a representative of the rent reduction meeting. He was the chairman of the meeting held on Rue Robert yesterday, but he advised the rickshaw drivers to wait patiently for a solution and not to take any out-of-bounds actions, and organized a persuasion team to persuade the rickshaw drivers to resume work at 9 a.m. this morning. There were police detectives and newspaper reporters at the scene to witness this. As for the leaflets, I don't know about them, I think they were fabricated by villains. When questioned, the other four, Zhu Fengxiang and others, only admitted to being representatives of the rent reduction meeting and denied sabotage. Finally, Gu Songmao, a member of the Car Dealers Association, complained about the situation. After Zhan Liangce presented the verified confession, he ordered Zheng and the other five to be taken back into custody and to be interrogated again in seven days.

Su Farmers Bank

Promoting Cooperative Sales 168

Sending Personnel to Organize Associations in Various Places

Planning to Establish Sales Branches

The Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank, in view of the fact that rural finance has been exhausted and the economy has collapsed in various places in recent years, the biggest reason is that the agricultural products of various places are stagnant in the countryside and cannot be directly transported and sold to major cities. If we can find a way to facilitate transportation and sales, then rural finance can be circulated and circulated immediately, and farmers' income can be increased invisibly. Therefore, the bank has recently been actively promoting cooperative transportation and sales and has spared no effort. Since the opening of the Shanghai "Cooperative Agricultural Products Transportation and Sales Office" of the bank this spring, it has received commissions from cooperative societies and other organizations in various places almost every day to transport and sell rice, wheat, cotton yarn, native cloth, daylily, and purchase bean cake, fertilizer, diesel, etc. Recently, it has also tried to act as an agent for livestock transportation and sales. Danyang, Qingjiangpu, Jingjiang, and Jintan have each entrusted batches of pigs to the office for transportation to Shanghai for sale. The procedures are simple and the results are quite good. According to the investigation of the Transportation and Sales Office, the selling price of rice, wheat, etc. transported and sold by farmers in various places as agents in the past is 30 cents to 50 cents higher per dan than the selling price near the towns in the place of origin, excluding transportation costs. According to the bank's calculation, if it acts as an agent for farmers to transport and sell 2 million dan of agricultural products this year, then the farmers in the province can invisibly increase their income by more than one million yuan this year. This kind of pioneering cooperative business has had remarkable results during the bank's trial period. It is heard that the bank has recently been more aggressive and has dispatched many investigators to designated business areas throughout the province to earnestly advocate organization and strive to promote various agricultural product transportation and sales cooperatives in order to expand the transportation and sales business. Those that have been established include the cotton production and sales cooperatives in Jiading, Changyinsha, Yancheng, and Funing, and the daylily production and sales cooperative and soybean production and sales cooperative in Suqian. Most of the other credit cooperatives that have a relationship with the Farmers Bank also兼operate in production and sales. At the same time, the bank is making every effort to expand agricultural warehouses in various places as a supplement to the transportation and sales business. It is also heard that the bank is planning to establish branches of the "Jiangsu Provincial Cooperative Agricultural Products Transportation and Sales Office" in important grain distribution centers in the province in order to connect with the Shanghai Transportation and Sales Office and effectively seek benefits for farmers in various places.

Delay of Various Trains: The No. 301 Shanghai-Beiping joint transportation express through train started from Beining Railway Beiping at 3:05 p.m. and arrived at Jinpu Railway Bengbu Station at 4:19 p.m. the day before yesterday. It arrived at Nanjing Station of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway at 9 a.m. yesterday morning. It did not arrive at Shanghai North Station until 4:40 p.m. yesterday, a delay of nine hours.

Within the scope of the Customs, there is only a distinction between Chinese and foreigners, and there is no public reason to speak of. Thieves hate their masters, which is not false. The three points mentioned above are just to defend against the sections mentioned in the letter. It is not easy to seek skin from a tiger, but our association is confident that the principle that Chinese people should serve as crew members on Customs patrol boats cannot be overthrown by any frivolous discussion. If it is said that the current crew members are full, then many of the members used by your office do not meet the qualifications of crew members and should be dismissed. As for the patrol boats currently being built in the dock, there are several more, and our association's proposal should be adopted to eliminate them and legally employ Chinese people. We should no longer use one-sided words to justify the crimes of concealment and protection. Our association's heart is to do good with others. If there is a change of heart, we will not overdo it. Correspondingly, we send this letter and ask you to check and see the reply for your荷

The Urgent Need for Disaster Relief in Jiangsu and Anhui Provinces 176

The China Relief Society recently received a telegram from Xu Saijia, director of the Jiangpu County Relief Center, stating: "Jiangpu has unfortunately suffered a devastating drought. Over 80% of the county has been affected. Ponds are dry, the countryside is cracked, and thousands of acres of fertile land have become scorched earth. The disaster is truly rare. Moreover, Jiangpu is known for its poverty, and farmers have little savings. Young adults are seeking a living and flocking to the city, while the elderly and weak beg for food and gather in the streets. What will young children do? Therefore, a temporary shelter for child victims has been established to provide accommodation and prevent them from becoming vagrants. However, funding is extremely tight, and this extraordinary disaster has further exacerbated the difficulty. How can we expand further? But since we are saving the lives of child victims, can we ignore their plight? Therefore, this special telegram is sent to request your generous assistance in providing relief funds and distributing charity grain. We eagerly await your response." Furthermore, according to a letter from Mr. Fu Erkan of the Congren Bureau in Anhui Province: "Anhui has not seen rain for two months since the beginning of summer. The land is cracked, and crops are withered. The drought is widespread, with people fleeing everywhere. The situation is dire. Moreover, after years of disaster and famine, and at a time when the rural economy is collapsing, the land is barren for miles. Is there anyone left alive? Now, in the villages, the elderly and weak are committing suicide daily. The situation is appalling and indescribable. There is nowhere to find food, and the future is bleak. Moreover, after a major disaster, epidemics often occur, and people die in piles. It is heartbreaking to witness. Therefore, I briefly report the circumstances and beg you to quickly organize relief efforts and widely publicize them, so that many hands can lighten the burden. If you have any medicine, please donate generously to help treat the disaster area." Based on these reports, the association faces a sluggish market and rural bankruptcy. Relief funds are depleted, and sighs are the only response. What good is it to just call out for help? However, 2,000 bottles of medicine have been allocated to be sent to Anhui to treat illnesses. The hungry are crying for food, and their lives are hanging by a thread. We can only appeal on their behalf, hoping that compassionate and kind people will lend a helping hand.

Page 13

Poisons Still Pervade

Two Red Pill Manufacturing Sites Uncovered 178

Two establishments broken up consecutively on Tiantong Road

Owners Liu Deji and Huang Yuchu arrested

Zhou Honglin, Chief Investigator of the General Inspectorate of the General Police Department, learned that Cantonese men He Yucheng and Chen Awu were specializing in the sale of red pills. He ordered his officers to contact He and Chen, stating that each bag of 1,000 red pills should be sold for seven dollars. It was agreed to purchase ten bags, totaling seventy dollars. A deposit of thirty dollars was paid in advance, and the remaining balance was to be paid at Room 1, Changhua Hotel, Fujian Road, the day before yesterday. The red pills were to be delivered at the same time. At the appointed time, Chief Investigator Zhou immediately reported to Western Detective Chief Bai Po and collaborated with Chinese Detective Chief Song Bingzheng and Detective Bao Xie Futang to wait in ambush. However, He and Chen did not deliver the goods until 4:00 AM the day before yesterday, when they finally delivered ten bags of red pills, totaling 10,000 pills. They were immediately arrested by the detectives. Under questioning, He confessed that the manufacturing site was located upstairs at 47 Tiantong Road, Hongkou, at Baoguang Hospital, and the owner was Cantonese man Huang Zhen. The detectives went to the address, arrested Huang, and seized a large box of red pills, approximately 50,000 to 60,000 pills, as well as numerous raw materials and machinery for making red pills. They also found over one hundred dollars in banknotes in Huang's pockets and wallet, all proceeds from the sale of red pills. Among them were two ten-dollar bills and two five-dollar bills, which were the deposit paid by the police. The bills had been secretly marked. Huang also confessed that another manufacturing site was located upstairs at 415 Beijiangxi Road, Tiantong Road. The detectives continued the search and seized 324 taels of red pills, numerous raw materials, and machinery, and arrested worker Liu Shuisheng. Under questioning, he confessed that the owners of this den were Cantonese men Liu Deji and Huang Yuchu. They then went to 78 Tiantong Road and arrested Liu and Huang. They also learned that Deng Wencao, who resided at 117 on the same road, was also a shareholder, and he was arrested as well. In total, seven suspects were arrested, and approximately 100,000 red pills, as well as numerous raw materials and machinery, were seized. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One. Police lawyer Gan Jingxian presented the case, prosecuted under Article 6 of the Anti-Opium Law, and requested severe punishment. However, he requested leniency for He Yucheng, as his confession had led to the case being solved. Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, questioned each defendant in detail and announced that the debate on the case was concluded, and the verdict would be announced next Thursday morning. The defendants were returned to custody.

Altering Checks and Forging Stamps

Embezzling Huge Sum of 30,000 Yuan 179

The Money Shop Joint Reserve Deceived

Relationship with Zifeng Money Shop

The Money Shop Joint Reserve at 112 Xingcheng Lane, Ningbo Road, is an organization formed by various money shops in the city, specializing in the payment of funds for each shop. Each shop receives a check from the reserve. The check number issued to the Zifeng Money Shop at 5 Fucheng Lane, Tianjin Road, was number 59, while the check number issued to Baofeng Fuji Money Shop, which was affiliated with Zifeng, was number 71. On the 6th of this month, a man suddenly presented a check with number 71 of Baofeng, stamped with a seal, and withdrew 30,000 yuan in banknotes from the reserve. The reserve paid the money. However, it was later discovered that the check had been altered from Zifeng's number 59, and the Baofeng seal was forged. The reserve reported the incident to the General Police Department, requesting an investigation. The captain ordered Chinese Detective Chief Li Yidong and Detectives Geng Debiao and Huang Fusen to investigate. The detectives found that the banknotes issued by the reserve were all new ten-yuan and five-yuan notes from the Central Bank. The front of the notes had a red "泉" (Fountain) mark, and the back had a black "心" (Heart) mark. They investigated based on this point. It was found that a Shaoxing man named Li Jinshou deposited 4,000 yuan of banknotes with the above-mentioned marks at the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank on Ningbo Road at 4:00 PM on the 6th of this month. His occupation and address were listed as an employee of the Zifeng Money Shop. The detectives went to Zifeng the day before yesterday and arrested Li, bringing him back to the police station. Under questioning, he claimed that the money was given to him by his aunt for deposit, but he could not describe his aunt's appearance or address, only saying that she was a laundress. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One. Police lawyer Gan Jingxian stated that the police were conducting a careful investigation into the inside story of the case and requested that the defendant be detained for investigation. Judge Qian Hongye questioned Li and approved his detention for one week. The content of the case is extremely complex. Once the truth is found, there will be many involved.

Approved by the Ministry of Communications

Rebuilding a Ten-Story Building for the Telegraph Office 180

Funded by the Postal Savings Bureau

Construction to begin in early next month

The Shanghai Telegraph Office of the Ministry of Communications plans to rebuild a new-style ten-story building on its original site at the intersection of Sichuan Road and Fuzhou Road, as the existing building is old. The site has an area of 1.97 mu and is the office's own property. In addition to a portion for its own use, the building will also house all Shanghai-based agencies affiliated with the Ministry of Communications for convenience. The plan has been approved by the Ministry of Communications, and all designs and models have been made. However, due to unresolved funding, it has been delayed until now. It is now learned that the funding has been invested by the Shanghai Postal Savings Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, so funding is no longer an issue. During the reconstruction period, the telegraph office will find another suitable location near the original site to connect the landlines and continue operations as usual. It is said that construction will officially begin in early next month.

Railway Bureau and Nanjing City

Handling Passenger Intermodal Transportation 181

Intermodal transportation contract signed yesterday

Intermodal passenger tickets valid for two days

The Nanjing Municipal Railway Administration sent personnel to negotiate intermodal passenger transportation with the Railway Bureau in September last year. It was initially planned to trial intermodal transportation of third and fourth-class passengers and baggage first. The Traffic Department and the Administration have now agreed on fourteen contract terms, which were formally signed yesterday (August 11). The full text is as follows:

Intermodal Transportation Contract 182

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration and the Nanjing Municipal Railway Administration, intermodal transportation contract. (1) The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration and the Nanjing Municipal Railway Administration (hereinafter referred to as the Administration) have entered into this agreement to facilitate third and fourth-class passenger traffic between the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and the Nanjing Municipal Railway. (2) The scope of the intermodal transportation is limited to third and fourth-class passengers and their baggage. The Administration is responsible for transportation within the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, and the Administration is responsible for transportation within Nanjing. Both parties' trains will not directly cross over to transfer passengers and baggage. Passengers and baggage will transfer trains at Nanjing Xiaguan Station. (3) The intermodal transportation stations on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway are limited to Shanghai North Station, Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Danyang, Zhazhe, Zhenjiang, and Zhenjiang South Gate. (4) The intermodal transportation fares shall be calculated by combining the fares of the two railways, as listed in Schedule A. If either party changes its fares, the other party shall be notified one month in advance. (5) The intermodal transportation tickets shall be valid for two days.

Free Baggage 183

(6) The free baggage allowance, whether for third or fourth-class passengers, is 40 kilograms per ticket for both the Administration and the Administration. If the baggage exceeds the above weight, the fee within the Administration is 2.4 hao per 20 kilograms or fraction thereof per kilometer. Within the Administration, the fee is 4.5 fen per 40 kilograms or fraction thereof from Nanjing Station to Gulou Station, 6 fen to Guofu Station, and 7.5 fen to Zhongzheng Street. (7) The forms for the intermodal transportation tickets, baggage tickets, and other intermodal transportation forms shall be agreed upon by both parties. The intermodal transportation tickets shall be printed and used by the Administration, with the Administration bearing 90% of the cost and the Administration bearing 10%. The remaining forms shall be printed and used by both parties themselves. (8) The Administration shall deduct its share from the daily intermodal transportation revenue and submit the Administration's share to the Nanjing Station Master of the Administration by 10:00 AM the next morning, who shall issue a receipt. The Administration shall also compile a daily report, indicating the number of intermodal transportation tickets sold and the fares, and submit it to the Nanjing Station Master for forwarding to the Administration's Accounting Office. The Administration shall deduct its share from the intermodal transportation revenue and send the Administration's share, along with a report, to the Administration for verification each month.

Intermodal Business 184

(9) The total intermodal transportation revenue shall be reported by both parties each week. All ticket amounts shall be reconciled monthly. Before the 10th of each month, both parties shall exchange various intermodal transportation reports for the previous month (such as ticket sales reports and baggage dispatch reports) and verify them in detail. The Administration shall then prepare a settlement statement and deliver it to the Administration before the 24th of the same month. (10) Baggage from the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway to the Nanjing Municipal Railway shall be transported by the Administration's baggage handlers to the platform of the Xiaguan Station of the Administration. Baggage from the Nanjing Municipal Railway to the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway shall be transported by the Administration's baggage handlers to the platform of the Nanjing Station of the Administration. Each party's baggage handlers shall sign and count the baggage. The loading and unloading fee for each item shall be 4 fen, which shall be shared monthly by both parties according to the proportion of intermodal transportation revenue. (11) This contract shall be made in duplicate, with each Administration keeping one copy for compliance, and two additional copies shall be submitted by the Administration and the Administration for their respective verification. (12) This contract shall be effective from August 11, 1934, to August 10, 1935, for a trial period of twelve months. If both parties agree, it may be continued for another twelve months. If either party does not intend to continue, it must notify the other party one month before the expiration of the contract. Failure to notify one month in advance shall be deemed as an agreement to continue the intermodal transportation. (13) Any matters not covered in this contract may be supplemented or amended with the consent of both parties through consultation. (14) This contract shall take effect from the date of signing.
