Japanese Department Store Bankrupt

Beifu Store Closes Down 186

Due to the Impact of the Shanghai Incident

According to the Japanese newspaper Mainichi Shimbun, the Beifu Department Store at the corner of Minhang Road and Miller Road suddenly closed down on the 9th. The store was operated by Kakuta Yoshitaro, president of Shanghai Xingye Co., Ltd., and was one of the largest stores selling Japanese goods in Shanghai. After the completion of the second Kakuta Building at the end of Showa 7 (two years ago), several rooms on the ground floor were used as a shopping mall. Since its opening, the number of customers has been increasing day by day. It was originally planned to expand business and move to the first Kakuta Building at the corner of Wen Road and Wusong Road, but the planned plan has been abandoned. The reason for the closure is that the glass factory operated by Kakuta on Yokohama Road, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, was destroyed during the Shanghai Incident, with losses of over one million yuan. After requesting direct damage certificates from the government, the relief funds allocated by the government were very small. The allocation rate was higher for those with less damage, and those with losses of over 5,000 yuan were disproportionately affected. Therefore, not only is it difficult for the glass industry to recover, but also the plans for revitalizing various aspects have been completely disappointed. In order to settle the debts for the revitalization, the store had to be closed. If the relief funds and existing goods are insufficient for disposal, the land base of the first Kakuta Building at the corner of Wusong Road and Wen Road will be sold. It is said that Kakuta's concern for property and credit is indeed a last resort.

Strangulation of a Child

Family Claims Body 187

For Eighteen Copper Coins

Suspicion Falls on a Monk

Yesterday (the 11th) morning, according to Cheng Youyu, a native of Danyang, together with Xu Shiying, the land guard of Shuangzi Thirteenth Ward, reported to the District Court that he was operating a sesame cake shop in Beida Street, Zhenru Town. He had parents in his hometown and a younger brother named Xiao Fugeng, who was fifteen years old this year. Xiao Fugeng came to Shanghai two years ago. Because of his young age, he had nothing to do, so he went out every day to sell sesame cakes on the street to supplement the family income. On the 6th of this month, at around 7:00 PM, Xiao Fugeng asked a tea customer named Monk A at Zhang Amao's teahouse in Houjiang for eighteen copper coins that were owed for the sesame cakes, but to no avail. An argument ensued. Then, Monk A asked Xiao Fugeng to go with him to get the money. He left and never returned. Because Xiao Fugeng did not return for several days, they were searching for him everywhere. Today, according to various newspapers, the body of an unidentified male, only ten years old, who had been strangled to death, was found in a ditch behind Yangjiaqiao and Jinan New Village in Zhenru (about three miles away from Cheng Youyu's sesame cake shop). The reporters immediately investigated the scene and confirmed that it was Xiao Fugeng. Therefore, they requested a coffin with the land guard to transport the body back to their hometown for burial and to apprehend the murderer. Yang Ruxiu, the prosecutor, summoned them and approved the delivery of the body, ordering a thorough search for the murderer. It was learned that Monk A had disappeared without a trace after the incident. Zhang Amao, the owner of the teahouse, was summoned by the police station and ordered to provide bail. The case involves only eighteen copper coins, but a life was taken with cruel means. It is truly unjust.

Medical Group Meeting

Elephant Clam Monopoly and Soaring Prices 190

Elephant clams, a medicinal material, are produced in Zhang Village, Yin County, Zhejiang Province, and sold in Shanghai, Shandong, and other places. The price has been no more than 30 to 40 yuan for many years. Since the establishment of the Elephant Clam Marketing Cooperative in the area, all elephant clams produced in the area have been exclusively sold by the cooperative, and private sales are not allowed. Violators will be punished, resulting in a gradual increase in prices. This year, the cooperative has further restricted production. The method is to prohibit the harvesting of elephant clams that should be unearthed in mid-April, abandoning them underground, resulting in Shanghai prices soaring to over 300 yuan per dan. Wang Yuandao Guoyao Pharmacy and Guo Hefan wrote to the National Medical Association, asking for joint efforts to stop this, so as to alleviate the burden on patients and prevent other drugs from doing the same. The National Medical Association referred it to the Special Committee for discussion. A meeting was held last night, attended by Guo Boliang, Zhang Zanchen, Sheng Xinru, Huang Baozhong, Lu Shie, Xia Zhongguang, Fu Yongyan, He Yunsheng, Yang Yanhe, Shen Xinjia, Cen Binghuan, Cen Zhiliang, Shi Jiqun, Ding Zhongying, Ren Nongxuan, Cheng Diren, Ding Jiwan, Xue Wenyuan, Xie Liheng, Yan Cangshan, Jiang Wenfang, Chinese National Medical Association, Shenzhou National Medical Association, Shanghai National Medical Association, and the Chinese Pharmaceutical Association, all represented by delegates. Jiang Wenfang was elected chairman. All agreed that this kind of unreasonable artificial price increase would greatly increase the burden on patients. If the producing areas of various important Chinese medicines followed suit, it would further undermine the prosperity of Chinese medicine and Chinese medicine. It was decided on the spot: (1) Send a letter to the cooperative questioning the following points: 1. What is the cost per dan of elephant clams for farmers in the producing area? 2. What is the production volume of the cooperative over the years, and what is the production and sales situation this year? 3. Does the cooperative consider the contract signed with the Chinese Pharmaceutical Association, etc., to be valid? 4. The price of elephant clams in Shanghai has risen to over 300 yuan per dan. Does the cooperative have any way to suppress the price? (2) Study alternative drugs for elephant clams to reduce the burden on patients. Lu Shie, Shi Jiqun, Cheng Diren, He Yunsheng, and Jiang Wenfang were invited to undertake the research. (3) Secret. (4) Secret. During the meeting, representatives of various groups expressed their determination to use the most effective methods to rationalize the price of elephant clams, so that both patients and medicinal farmers would benefit.

The Shanghai Municipal National Medicine Association formulated regulations for establishing a medical school and sent a letter requesting research and reply for approval and implementation. It was resolved that it should be handed over to the Special Committee for research. 5. Mr. Guo Boliang sent a gift of longevity as a foundation for the construction of the association building, totaling 1,500 yuan. How to keep the money was resolved. It was handed over to Mr. Xue Wenfang for temporary collection and transfer to the Fundraising Committee. 6. How to express the appreciation for Mr. Guo Boliang's donation was resolved. It was decided to publish an advertisement of gratitude, and the Secretariat was asked to handle it at its discretion. (C) Temporary motions: Committee member Xia Zhongguang proposed to apply to the Health Bureau for re-examination of licenses for business purposes. Change of General Manager of the World Book Company 196

Shen Zhifang Replaced as Supervisor

The 13th Annual General Meeting of Shareholders of the World Book Company's head office on Dalian Bay Road in this city was convened on July 29. In addition to passing important resolutions, the election of directors and supervisors was held. The results of the ballot were as follows: The elected directors were Li Shizeng, Wu Yunzhai, Wang Yiting, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Jingjiang, Qian Xinzhi, Du Chongyuan, Chu Minyi, Lu Zhongliang, Jin Zhaoyan, Li Shuhua, Chen Hexian, Cui Zhuxi, Shen Zhifang, and Lu Gaoyi, totaling fifteen people. The elected supervisors were Wu Zhihui, Li Linyu, and Qi Zhongqing, totaling three people. The elected directors and supervisors of the company are mostly well-known figures of the time. This was reported in this newspaper on July 30. It is reported that the bureau held its first board meeting on the second floor of the General Distribution Office on Fuzhou Road on the 5th of this month and publicly elected Mr. Zhang Jingjiang as chairman of the board, and Li Shizeng, Wu Yunzhai, and Cui Zhuxi as executive directors. It is known that the book bureau was founded single-handedly by Mr. Shen Zhifang in the tenth year of the Republic. The initial scale was small, but in a few years, the business was quite extensive and developed rapidly. Shen devoted all his efforts to the company and made it one of the three major companies. In thirteen years, it has achieved such a scale. There is no other cultural undertaking that has risen to the same level. Recently, Mr. Shen, feeling that his age was increasing and his energy was declining, and he was overwhelmed by the heavy tasks, wrote to the board of directors requesting resignation. After deliberation by the board of directors, and facing Shen's insistence on resigning, it was decided to reluctantly grant approval after considering Shen's hard work for the company for more than ten years. It was also decided that Mr. Lu Gaoyi, the company's manager, should concurrently serve as general manager, and that Mr. Shen should be hired as the company's supervisor, working in the head office as usual. Both proposals were unanimously passed by the board of directors. It is reported that the company's board's announcement and letter of appointment were sent out yesterday (the 11th). On the same afternoon, the company's authorities convened a meeting of all colleagues. Executive Director Cui Zhuxi, Supervisor Wu Zhihui, and others all came to deliver speeches. Supervisor Shen Zhifang and Acting General Manager Lu Gaoyi both gave sincere speeches. Many colleagues also gave earnest speeches (the length of the speeches is omitted). The atmosphere of harmony and talent was prosperous.

Sailors Rescued by the Hairui Steamer

Are Boatmen from the Sinking Tongchangyuan Ship 197

The Shandong Yizhou Prefecture Shijiuzhai Tongfeng Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Company recently loaded a large quantity of raw peanuts and raw oil, and sent four large sandboats to Shanghai. Among them, the Tongchangyuan sandboat was loaded with 200 bags of raw peanuts and 470 baskets of raw oil. It set sail at the same time as the three sandboats. The cargo on the Tongchangyuan ship was sent to Shanghai and delivered to the Senmao Company at Guanquai in Nanshi. After setting sail, at 5 a.m. on Tuesday, it encountered a hurricane on the Lvsi sea. When turning the boat, a large wave hit and sank the bow of the boat. Two more waves came, and the boat capsized. The fourth wave broke the sandboat, and all the cargo and boatmen fell into the sea. The area is located on the Dashachang sea, north of Sheshan. At that time, the China Merchants Bureau's Hairui steamer happened to sail to the Lvsi sea. At that time, the second mate Yang Biru was on duty. The helmsman first saw people drifting on the sea and reported to the chief mate Qian Yujia. Qian immediately ordered the ship to stop and lower the gangplank to the sea. He rescued two people holding on to the mast onto the ship. Six people were found holding on to broken wooden boards at the bow of the ship and were also rescued. It was said that there were still seven people in the sea. The sampan searched for two hours but did not find them. They had probably drowned. The rescued people had been drifting for two days and two nights without food. Their bodies were pale. If they had not been rescued, they would have died. The ship provided them with drinks, clothes, and medical treatment. Among them was Sun Xinhe, 65 years old, nicknamed Xiaotian, who was the owner of the Tongchangyuan sandboat. He kowtowed to the ships. Sun said that he had been sailing this sandboat for 39 years. This time, he loaded cargo to Shanghai, and was sunk by the strong wind. He did not take anything from the boat, only the statue of the Goddess of the Sea. The other seven people must have died. The three ships traveling with them are also likely to have met with misfortune. At about 7 a.m. yesterday morning, after the Hairui entered the port, Chief Mate Qian Yujia took Sun Xiaotian to the bureau to see Zhao Yuntai, the head of the Ship Section. After Zhao inquired about the cause, he gave him five yuan and sent someone to accompany him to the Navigation Administration Bureau to ask for a discretionary decision. After the Navigation Administration Bureau inquired about the cause of the accident, it notified the cargo owner to find a way to send the people back to Shandong. The Tongchangyuan sandboat lost a total of two or three thousand yuan, including cargo, sailors' money, and clothes. Sun Xiaotian and others are now reporting to the Senmao Company in Nanshi, which purchased and transported the goods, and reporting the cause of the accident to the Tongfeng Company in Yizhou, Shandong.

Fu Xiao'an Sues Yan Dajue 198

Japanese Consulate Orders Dai Zhenwu to Repay Debt

Fu Decides to Appear in Court at Next Hearing

The case of Fu Xiao'an, chairman of the Bank of China, suing lawyer Yan Dajue for intimidation in connection with the debt owed by Dai Zhenwu, a Ningbo native who has become a Japanese citizen, has attracted considerable attention in society. It is now known that the debt was borrowed from the Hongkou branch of the Bank of China in the twentieth year of the Republic. After the due date, Dai repeatedly delayed and refused to pay. Zhu Huanwen, the manager of the branch, filed a lawsuit with the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai as the legal representative to demand payment. Dai made many excuses during the court hearing, but the judge ruled that the evidence was conclusive and did not allow for excuses. Dai's empty claims were insufficient, and a judgment was issued on the 27th of last month, ordering Dai Zhenwu to repay the full amount. During the litigation, Dai entrusted a certain gentleman from Ningbo to mediate unsuccessfully. Later, he entrusted lawyer Yan to send a letter to Fu, alleging that the letter not only fabricated facts but also contained intimidation. Therefore, he hired lawyer Dai Chengxiang to file a private prosecution with the First Special District Court. The case has now been adjourned to the 17th of this month for continued hearing. It is reported that Mr. Fu Xiao'an will personally appear in court at that time.

Zhengji Company

Hongli Runs Aground Off Dengzhou 199

Company Says It Escaped Danger Long Ago and Is Being Repaired in Dalian

Previous Rumors of Grounding May Be Misinformation

Xinsheng News Agency reports that Zhengji Shipping Company's Hongli, with a gross tonnage of 771 tons and a net tonnage of 602 tons, specializes in sailing to Yingkou, Andong, Longkou, Yantai, and other places. Yesterday, according to news from the shipping industry, the ship ran aground on reefs when sailing to the Dengzhou sea the day before yesterday, due to a hurricane. Xinsheng News Agency reporters went to Zhengji Company last night and learned that the Hongli ran aground near Dengzhou a week ago after loading cargo from Yantai. It was rescued and escaped danger, but the bottom of the ship was damaged, so it sailed to Dalian for repairs in the shipyard. The company did not receive any telegrams from Dalian or Yantai about this grounding. It is feared that it is a misunderstanding of the previous grounding, as the ship is probably still being repaired in Dalian.

Publication of Yuan Zhonglang's "Bathing Flower Studio Collection" 201

The "Bathing Flower Studio Collection" was written by Yuan Hongdao (Shi Gong) of the late Ming Dynasty and was one of the books destroyed during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. Su Changgong's laughter, anger, and scolding all became articles. Shi Gong deeply understood the secret and was a strong general in the naturalistic literary movement of the late Ming Dynasty. He is also the most fashionable type of writing in the current literary world, the so-called Yuan Zhonglang school. Because it is a banned book, there are very few copies circulating. Many literati in China may not know who Yuan Zhonglang is, or what kind of writing Yuan Zhonglang's writing is. They must want to be the first to read it, so it is specially reprinted to supply readers. It is now distributed by the Times Book Company. The book is a reprint of the original manuscript from the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty, so it is no different from the original. The binding is excellent, easy to carry, and the value is cheap.

Pudong Kidnapping Case

Female Bandit Watching the Ticket Escorted to Court 203

Chen Fengxiang, the deceased director of Tudong in Pudong, was quite wealthy, which made him coveted by a general gang of bandits. At about 10 p.m. on July 10 of this year, Chen's son, Chen Baoming (16 years old), was kidnapped by bandits. That night, Baoming took advantage of the bandits' deep sleep and escaped from the den of thieves, returning home safely. Afterwards, Dong Zhaocheng, the director of the Third Section of the Third District in charge, found the bandits' nest in Hujiazhai, Situ, Haili Township, Nanhui County. He secretly ordered patrol officer Li Cunzheng to lead the police there quietly the day before yesterday. With the cooperation of the police chief of the Second Branch of Zhoupu, they arrested the woman Hu Yao, who was watching over the ransom, and a suspect living with her, inside No. 69 Hujiazhai, Situ. They were escorted to the station. After interrogation, it was learned that the suspect was not related and was immediately released on bail. Hu Yao was immediately sent to the Third Section of the Main Bureau. Hu Yao claimed to be 43 years old, from Nanhui County, living in Hujiazhai. Her former husband was dead, and she remarried to Hu Hegen as her husband. One night, my husband and I were already asleep when Li Apei came to knock on the door. I got up to open the door, and saw three people in total, one was Li Apei, one was not recognized, and there was a sixteen- or seventeen-year-old child. Li Apei claimed that he was tired from walking and came here to rest for a while, and told me to go to sleep and not to be next to him, so I went to sleep, and I didn't know anything else. As for Li Apei, he used to open an egg shop in Jinhui Bridge, Pudong, and my husband sold eggs for a living, so they knew each other. After being interrogated yesterday, he immediately prepared a document and ordered the police to transfer Hu Yao to the local court for legal action. After a long investigation by the prosecutor, he ordered her to be detained pending interrogation.

A Woman's Corpse at the Wusong Fort 204

Eight Knife Wounds to the Head

Body Moved to the Roadside After Death

A wounded female corpse was found on the roadside east of the coast guard post at Wusong Fort yesterday morning. The corpse was about 20 years old, with short hair and dressed in a black Indian silk cheongsam. After investigation by the guard police, it was reported to the Seventh District of the Public Security Bureau. Yao, the District Chief, sent people to investigate. It was found that the female corpse had eight powerful wounds to the head. However, no bloodstains were found next to or near the corpse, so it was determined that she was murdered and moved to the roadside. It was probably transported by car to the roadside and abandoned there. District Chief Yao, considering the matter related to murder, ordered the local officials to report it to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy in order to arrest the murderer and investigate the case.

Two Slaps and a Life 205

Yang Shulin Commits Suicide After Being Humiliated

Yang Shulin, a native of Jiangxi, 37 years old, lived at No. 21 Dasheng Lane, Xiaodongshou. He borrowed more than 50 yuan from his relative Yang Dongsheng due to urgent needs. He has not yet been able to repay it due to economic difficulties. At about 1 p.m. the day before yesterday, Dongsheng went to Yang's house to demand repayment. The debt was not paid, and a major conflict arose between the two sides. At that time, Dongsheng was furious and slapped Yang twice. The neighbors mediated and resolved the matter. However, Yang was humiliated and depressed, and had the idea of committing suicide. At about 12 p.m. that night, he secretly untied his belt and hanged himself under the attic at home. It was not until about 5 a.m. yesterday morning that he was discovered by his housemate. But Yang had been dead for a long time, and it was impossible to revive him. They immediately reported the situation to the head of the Second Section of the First District, Liu. After hearing the report, Liu ordered the local officials to report to the Shanghai Local Court to send someone for an autopsy because the matter involved human life.

Apprentice Painter Falls to Death 206

Tragedy of Painting the Roof of the Special Second Court

A three-story Western-style house at No. 16 Xuehuali Road, French Concession, is the property of the French Bureau of Public Works. It used to be the residence of the Western Prison Warden. After the prison of the Public Hall was taken back, the uppermost floor of the house was used by the Judicial Consultant's Office to set up an office and a lawyer's office in the police station. The second floor and the bottom floor were lent to the Special Second Local Court. The seventh and eighth courts were set up on the bottom floor. The second floor was set up by the Judicial Sergeant and the bailiffs. The roof was covered with lead skin and had to be painted once a year in summer. Recently, Wu Shengtai Paint Shop at No. 297 Fuxu Road was hired to send craftsmen to paint the roof. At 6:20 p.m. the day before yesterday, when the work was about to stop, Liu Afang, a 19-year-old apprentice painter from Shaoxing, slipped and fell from the roof, falling to the side of the road, causing internal organ and brain injuries. Xie Zhiming, a Chinese policeman No. 707 on guard in front of the Special Second District Prison, saw this and reported it to the Lujiawan Police Station. Liu was sent to Guangci Hospital in a car, but he died of serious injuries before he could be treated. His body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Mortuary for an autopsy. His father, Liu Sijiu, was sent to the case by a detective. The next morning, the Special Second Local Court appointed Prosecutor Wang Ren to the mortuary along with a forensic doctor and a clerk to verify that the deceased died from falling injuries during his lifetime. He ordered the body to be handed over to the father of the deceased, Liu Sijiu, for burial.

Summary of Bank Inspection Reports 208

The Central Bank's 205th Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states: This association is responsible for inspecting the bank's issuance of convertible currency reserves, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. We held the 205th inspection at the bank's Issuance Bureau on August 10, 23rd year of the Republic. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible currency issued is 75,513,068 silver yuan, including 69,135,568 silver yuan in silver certificates and 6,377,500 yuan in fractional currency certificates. The total amount of convertible currency reserves is 75,513,068 yuan, including 61,899,068 yuan in cash reserves. The cash reserves include 58,539,791 yuan stored in the bank's issuance treasury, 1,571,751 yuan stored in branches in various ports, and 1,787,526 yuan stored in peer banks. The guarantee reserves are equivalent to 13,614,000 silver yuan. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible currency issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible currency reserves is 373,324.70 yuan. The reserves include 7,351 taels, 9 maces, and 5 fen of standard gold, equivalent to 373,324.70 yuan of customs gold at a fixed price of 50779. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Currency Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the amount of cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is specially made. August 11, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mingdong, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiqing.

The China Reclamation Bank's Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: The China Reclamation Bank's issuance treasury and business treasury have always been completely separated. According to the bank's regulations, cash reserves are above 70% and guarantee reserves are below 30%. On the 11th of this month, the accountant Tu Zikang, together with the representatives of the board of directors and supervisors Xu Jiqing and Xu Busun, inspected the results as follows: The exchange coupon issuance continued to be 6,958,000 silver yuan, and the total amount of exchange coupon reserves was 6,958,000 silver yuan, including 4,946,000 silver yuan in cash reserves and 2,012,000 silver yuan in guarantee reserves. 22nd year of the Republic of China

General Business Conditions of Major Chinese Banks 212

Compiled by the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China, Published Yesterday

The "Study of the General Business Conditions of Major Chinese Banks in the 22nd Year of the Republic of China" compiled by the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China has now been published. This book is a sequel to the "Study of the General Business Conditions of Major Chinese Banks in the Last Ten Years." The original book made a comprehensive historical comparison and analysis of the business conditions of thirty major Chinese banks from the 10th to the 20th years of the Republic of China, serving as the only reliable source of information and statistics for studying China's banking industry. This book focuses specifically on a more detailed study of the business conditions of major banks in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, with the figures for the 20th and 21st years of the Republic of China also listed in detail to provide readers with clear convenience. It truly has independent value from the original book and is an indispensable book for those studying the banking industry. It was published and graciously presented to us yesterday, and we are writing this to express our gratitude and introduce it to readers.

Zheng Zhaojia Defeats Watanabe 222

Watanabe's momentum is strong Watanabe is the 15th-ranked singles player in Japan last year, and his tennis skills are similar to Zheng Zhaojia. However, his lack of endurance was unexpected. His shots were very powerful. After Watanabe served and won a game each at the beginning of the match, Watanabe relied on his fierce left and right diagonal shots to win four consecutive games, leading 5-1. Zhaojia repeatedly tried to block the net, but all failed. Sometimes the kill shot was too light, and sometimes it was hit out of bounds. By the seventh game, Zhaojia repeatedly attacked his backhand, winning a game. Watanabe won the first set 6-2.

Zhaojia comes from behind Zhaojia's loss in the first set was due to unstable shots. From the second set, Watanabe won two consecutive games. After several equalities in the second game, Watanabe won. In the third game, Watanabe served, and Xiao Zheng attacked his backhand again, finally winning the game. Unexpectedly, after this fierce battle, Watanabe's energy was exhausted. From then on, he was unable to recover, unable to run, and unable to hit hard. Xiao Zheng did whatever he wanted. Xiao Zheng won six consecutive games, taking back the second set 6-2. At the beginning of the third set, Xiao Zheng was careless and in great danger, trailing 1-4. A glimpse of Ota's tennis skills Today, what we saw of Ota's tennis skills may have been less impressive than three or four years ago. His hitting technique is not particularly moving, but his steadiness is rare, which is the reason for his victory. The forehand draw is the most powerful and his masterpiece. From beginning to end, he made long baseline draws and only went to the net once. Baohua's net performance yesterday won the praise of the audience, often putting Ota in a desperate situation. It is a pity that his shots were unstable, and his shots were not as good as Ota's, resulting in repeated self-destruction at the net, and most of the points were lost there. Compared with Ota, the difference is not far.

Baohua takes the lead twice In the first set, Ota won 9-7 after a fierce battle. When Baohua was 2-4 and 3-5, he tried his best to catch up to 5-5. Then, he exceeded Ota twice at 6-5 and 7-6, but unfortunately, he was defeated by Ota's three consecutive victories. Baohua served and won first. Ota also won the serve. Baohua's serve game was lost because of two double serve errors, so Ota took the lead again at 3-1. In the sixth game, Baohua once went to the net to block, but although he succeeded, he still lost the game. Lin repeatedly wanted to go to the net, but could not. When Lin served when he was behind 3-5 in the ninth game, he won a game with a fierce serve. Then the situation suddenly changed, and he won three consecutive games, taking the lead at 6-5. But in the next game, Ota won with a smooth game. Baohua scored three consecutive points and took the lead again at 7-6, but in the end, he failed to grasp the opportunity and lost three consecutive games to Ota, losing 7-9.

Ota wins steadily Lin still served at the beginning of the second set and won the first game. Ota turned around and took the lead again at 3-1. In the fifth game, Lin served and won with a heavy ball. In the next game, Lin took the opportunity to go to the net and succeeded, so it became 3-3. But in the seventh game, Lin's serve game was won by Ota, so it became 4-3 and 5-3, and the situation had spread. Ota relied on his steady hitting technique to win the second set 6-4 again.

Strengthening the Foundation for Enslaving Northeastern Youth

Required to Return to "Manchukuo" to Serve Within One Year

(Special Dispatch from Changchun, Northeast) In order to strengthen the foundation for enslaving Northeastern youth, Japan has ordered the puppet Ministry of Education to dispatch students to study at schools in Japan such as Tokyo Higher Normal School, Hiroshima Higher School, and Tamagawa Gakuen. These instructor students are outstanding teachers selected and recommended by the puppet Ministry of Education from various provinces, districts, and cities. Relief for Northeastern Students Studying Abroad

28,000 Remitted 238

(Nanjing, 11th) The methods for distributing relief funds for Northeastern students studying abroad have been determined: Publicly funded students will receive an annual subsidy of 1,800 yuan, while privately funded students will be divided into four grades with subsidies of 400, 600, 700, and 800 yuan, limited to one payment. The intention of these funds is to provide temporary relief. If a student is unable to sustain themselves even after receiving the subsidy, the funds will be used as travel expenses for their return to China. Currently, students from England, France, Germany, Italy, Belgium, and other countries have applied, and a total of 28,000 yuan has been remitted.

General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts to be Established 240

The preparatory office for the General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts is located at the Lizi Society in Nanjing. Since its establishment, it has been urging various provinces and cities to establish provincial boy scout councils, form boy scout troops, and carry out various boy scout-related tasks, all of which are generally in order. After the General Regulations of the Boy Scout Association were revised and approved by the Central Conference in August of last year, preparations were made to establish the General Association and build a clubhouse on Wutaishan in Nanjing. Due to financial difficulties, the project was suspended indefinitely. The issue of establishing the General Association was not urgently submitted for discussion at the preparatory meeting of the association. The original personnel in charge of preparations in Nanjing were Dai Chuanxian, Zhu Jiahua, Zhang Zhizhong, and others. There were also more than ten preparatory committee members. Regarding the affiliation of the association, its nature suggests it should belong to military training, but in practice, it involves students from various schools, so whether it belongs to the Directorate General of Military Training or the Ministry of Education has not been decided. Moreover, the personnel in charge of the association's preparations are highly respected, making the affiliation issue even more complicated. Recently, it seems that it has been assigned to the Ministry of Education. Last month, a proposal by the Ministry of Education to establish the Chinese Boy Scout Council was approved by the Central Committee. After the council appoints personnel, it will take over from the preparatory office of the Boy Scout General Association. The preparatory office of the Boy Scout General Association is now handling the closing procedures and preparing for the handover. The preparatory work is about to come to an end. The General Association is expected to be established this month or at the latest in September. It is also heard that the members of the Chinese Boy Scout Council were nominated by the Ministry of Education and approved by the Central Committee. Future council members will be elected by the boy scouts themselves.

Second Day of the Second Annual Meeting 241

Zeng Zhaolun and Two Others Elected as Candidates for Directors

Next Annual Meeting Tentatively Scheduled for Beijing, Qingdao, and Guangzhou

Papers Read This Morning, Annual Banquet Held This Evening

The second annual meeting of the Chinese Chemical Society was held yesterday, the second day of the opening. Over eighty members attended, including Chen Yuguang, Wu Chengluo, Shao Jialin, Zeng Zhaolun, Wu Haoran, Tang Yuanji, and others. The business meeting was held in the morning, a public banquet was held by various factories at noon, and a visit to major factories in the South Shanghai District was held in the afternoon. A public banquet was held at the Science Instrument Museum in the evening. Details are recorded as follows:

Business Meeting 242

The business meeting was held at 9:00 AM, chaired by Chen Yuguang and recorded by Wu Chengluo. A. Report Matters: (1) Report by Secretary Wu Chengluo, (2) Report by Accountant Tang Yuanji, (3) Report on Publications by Zeng Zhaolun and Dai Anbang, (4) Report on the Election of Directors by Chen Yuguang: Nine directors will serve a three-year term, with one-third of the directors being re-elected each year. The terms of the current directors Chen Yuguang, Wu Chengluo, and Wang Jin will expire in the 24th year [of the Republic, i.e. 1935]. The terms of Chen Kezhong, Ma Jie, and Huang Xinyan will expire in the 25th year [of the Republic, i.e. 1936], so there is no need for re-election. The terms of the other three directors, Zheng Zhenwen, Yao Wannian, and Zeng Zhaolun, have expired. According to regulations, a supplementary election was held, and Zeng Zhaolun, Zheng Zhenwen, and Pan Xudong were elected. (5) Annual Meeting Report by Shao Jialin.

Resolutions 243

(1) The permanent membership fees and entrance fees will be used as a foundation, and a foundation committee will be established. The resolution was passed. However, entrance fees may be used temporarily. Wu Chengluo, Zeng Zhaolun, Wu Haoran, Yang Gongshu, Li Linyu, Yang Chengxun, Wu Yun Chu, Huang Xinyan, and Fan Xudong were elected as foundation committee members. (2) The location of the next annual meeting was decided. It was resolved that the locations will be Beijing, Qingdao, and Guangzhou, to be selected by the board of directors. (3) Compiling chemistry magazines and books from various universities and research institutions for mutual application was resolved to be handled by the Chinese editorial department. (4) Editing a series of chemistry books was resolved to be handled by the chemistry book series committee. (5) Editing industrial chemistry textbooks was resolved to be handled by the chemistry book series committee. (6) The Chemical Society will take Chinese products as its subject, conduct systematic investigations, and conduct research on quality identification, utilization methods, or improvement of manufacturing. It was resolved to be discussed in detail by the board of directors. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Liu mentioned that students going abroad should pay attention to the following: First, bring fewer luggage items to avoid hassle; Second, book berths and dining table seats on the ship early and be careful with what you eat, avoiding overeating; Third, when customs inspects your luggage, avoid being overly polite or impolite, as either can cause trouble; Fourth, when boarding and disembarking trains, proceed in order; Fifth, for accommodation, it is best to stay with foreign families. If going to the United States, there are three places you must see: (1) American families, (2) American churches, (3) when returning home, it is best to travel through Europe. Cao mentioned that after studying for a year, you should conduct investigations in various places so that what you learn is practical. Those studying in Europe should pay particular attention to observing the social conditions of Europe. Song mentioned that there is a great shortage of specialized talent in the Chinese insurance industry, and he hopes that those with relevant skills will pay more attention and pursue further studies. Lu mentioned that if you do not have friends abroad, the YMCA can write letters of introduction on your behalf. He telegraphed the New York YMCA the other day, and they should send someone to the dock to take care of you if you have any trouble when you land in Seattle. Or you can seek help from the local YMCA, and they will definitely do their best to assist you.

Siming University Scholarship Realized 254

Yong Gentlemen Yu Qiaqing and Others Benefiting Future Generations

First Scholarship of 125 Places

Yu Qiaqing, Sun Hengfu, and other founders of Siming University have initiated a scholarship program, planning to implement it when school starts this fall. Details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now heard that a scholarship committee has been organized to take charge of the program, composed of the founders and organizers of Siming University. The committee members include Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Shouyong, Sun Hengfu, Zhou Junyan, Qin Runqing, Liu Hongsheng, Wang Boyuan, Hu Mengjia, Li Shuxiong, Liu Jisheng, Wei Bozhen, Wu Jingxiong, Zhang Shenzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Li Quanshi, Wu Zhihao, Li Gufan, Wu Yaqin, and Zheng Chengqing, totaling nineteen people. Wei Bozhen was elected as the director. The internal organization is divided into financial and audit groups. Qin Runqing was appointed as cashier and Li Shuxiong as accountant, each responsible for handling their respective affairs. It has now been decided that the first scholarship will be for 125 recipients, with each recipient receiving 400 yuan per year, requiring a total scholarship fund of 50,000 yuan. The full amount has been pledged by Sun Hengfu of Siming Bank, Yu Qiaqing of Sanbei Company, and Liu Hongsheng and Wang Boyuan. For the first year, Siming Bank will provide 25,000 yuan, Sanbei 5,000 yuan, and Yu Qiaqing, Liu Hongsheng, and Wang Boyuan will each provide 5,000 yuan. Li Shuxiong will provide 2,500 yuan, and Liu Jisheng and Wei Bozhen will each provide 1,250 yuan. The scholarship funds will be deposited in Siming Bank and disbursed in installments each semester. It is heard that the scholarship is open to students from Ningbo who have graduated from high school but cannot afford to attend university, those who have entered university but cannot afford to continue their studies, and those who have graduated from university but cannot afford to pursue graduate studies. Applications can be submitted starting from August 13th. In recent days, many students from Ningbo have been inquiring about the details through the Ningbo Native Place Association, and they are already overwhelmed with inquiries. It is expected that there will be even more applicants when the registration begins. It is also heard that the association plans to run the program for the first year and then continue for the second, third, and fourth years. It is estimated that by the fourth year, the scholarship will have 500 recipients, requiring an expenditure of 200,000 yuan. After the fourth year, the cycle will repeat, with 500 recipients each year. Such a large-scale scholarship program is unprecedented in the country.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Doubt and Reaction 256

— White Goose

Children! I believe you must have thrown coins or other things on the ground or on a table. After throwing them, what do you feel about the objects? Wouldn't they bounce up? And the harder you throw them, the higher they bounce, right? But have you ever wondered:

"Why is this happening?"

The British Newton doubted this phenomenon, and because of this doubt, he invented the law of "reaction," which means that when a coin is thrown onto a table or the ground, the table or the ground exerts an equal force in the opposite direction. Because the force exerted is equal, the harder you throw the coin, the higher it bounces. And because the direction is opposite, the coin is thrown downwards, and it bounces upwards.

Children! We should doubt everything, and you should ask: "Why is this happening?" I know that if you do this, your knowledge will improve rapidly, and becoming Newton and inventing laws is not a difficult thing.

The Lazy Watch 257

— Jūgāo

The wall clock said to the wristwatch, "We are working permanently without stopping, which is too hard. I have now come up with a way to get a long-term rest." The wristwatch asked, "What is the method?" The wall clock said, "From today onwards, we just need to run fast sometimes and slow sometimes. When the owner sees that the time we show is not accurate, he will definitely send us to the clock shop for repair. After the repair, we continue to do the same. After several repairs, the owner still can't get the accurate time. Then, the owner will be discouraged and give us a long-term rest." The wristwatch said, "This method is not very appropriate. Showing accurate time is our duty. People who abandon their duties and neglect their duties will never have good results, I think."

The wall clock saw that the wristwatch did not agree with its proposed method, and secretly laughed at its stupidity and timidity, so it went alone to do this. Sure enough, the owner sent it to the clock shop for repair. After three or four repairs in a row, it was still full of errors, and it was like not being repaired at all. The owner then threw it in the corner of the drawer. At this time, the wall clock, seeing that it had achieved its goal of a long-term rest, felt unspeakably happy in its heart.

Unexpectedly, things turned out contrary to the wall clock's expectation. It quietly lived in the corner of the drawer. Although it seemed very comfortable, it was covered in dust and lost its original beauty. The things that kept it company were all junk. It felt somewhat disappointed. But even more unfortunate things followed. The owner sent it to the clock shop to exchange for a new watch strap for the wristwatch. The clock shop owner saw that all its parts were rusted, so he unloaded it and used its parts to make up for the damage to other watches. As a result, the wall clock was torn apart, leaving only an empty shell. It deeply regretted it, but it was already too late.

Cicada! Cicada!

In this hot summer,

Singing leisurely melodies.

The enemy is laughing secretly;

But you can't wake up the dreams of those who believe in military force

Or the wild birds above.

Autumn wind is about to rise,

Have you prepared your provisions?

X X X X

In this kind of year,

In that kind of surrounding,

Why don't you bury your head in hard work,

But only keep shouting loudly;

"Cicada! Cicada!"

The Fierce and Cruel Second Brother Xia 259

— Yīzhèn

Old Uncle Nian has four children: First Sister Chun, Second Brother Xia, Third Sister Qiu, and Fourth Brother Dong. Chun and Qiu are the two most gentle and beautiful children, and everyone likes them and loves them. But the personalities of Second Brother Xia and Fourth Brother Dong are different from their sisters, and they are the two most inferior and naughty children. They are completely the typical bad children.

Fourth Brother Dong's face is always gloomy and terrifying. The children of the Hundred Herbs family will run away when they see him. The timid ones are scared to death by him. It is said that his two "guys" are very powerful; he can do Shaolin Kung Fu very well.

Second Brother Xia is a tyrannical child. He has no etiquette in dealing with people, and everyone hates and scolds him when they see him. He has thousands of retainers, like flies, mosquitoes, gnats, centipedes, snakes... All of them are cruel villains and insidious people.

Among these four children, Second Brother Xia is the most fierce and cruel: like this year, he forcibly occupied the home of "Yellow Mold," seized the power of "Rain" Old Gentleman, and dried up the water in the fields; causing the farmers great suffering!

Hiccup 260

— Bózhēn

The clock rang twelve times, as if saying, "It's time for people to eat lunch." Min'er felt very happy after hearing the clock strike twelve times, because his stomach had been rumbling with hunger for an hour or two. He ran like a flying arrow to the kitchen to tell his mother: "Mom! Is the rice cooked yet? It's already twelve o'clock." His mother said, "It's cooked. Go arrange the chairs and wipe the table clean. I'll put out the side dishes."

Min'er went outside to arrange the chairs and wipe the table, busy without stopping.

At the round table sat Min'er and his father, mother, and his older brother, Cong'er.

His mother had just given Min'er a bowl of rice. He took it and quickly put it into his mouth, not even chewing it carefully.

Unexpectedly, he started to hiccup. His mother patted him on the top of his head. He felt that his hiccups got a little better with each pat from his mother. Sure enough, after more than ten pats, the hiccups stopped. He said, "Mother is an effective doctor." His older brother laughed at what he said.

But Min'er didn't know why eating quickly caused hiccups, so he asked his older brother.

His older brother said, "There are two tubes in a person's throat. The one in the front is called the trachea, and the fresh air we breathe passes through this tube to the lungs. The one in the back is called the esophagus, and the food we eat passes through this tube to the stomach.

So why does eating quickly cause hiccups?

The rice we eat should normally go to the esophagus, but if we eat too fast, the rice doesn't have time to go to the esophagus and mistakenly enters the trachea.

At that time, you shouldn't swallow any more rice. Wait until the rice comes back out of the trachea and goes back to the esophagus, then your hiccups will stop."

So from then on, Min'er always chewed carefully every time he ate.

Children's Science Lecture

Thunder and Lightning 261

— Lin Yin

Little friends! When there are showers in the summer, you must hear the rumbling sounds in the sky and see the shimmering light. Your parents may have told you, "That's the Thunder God and Lightning Goddess performing magic, punishing all evildoers." You must not believe this. You should know that the sound is the result of air vibration, and the light is caused by the contact of electricity.

Clouds often contain electricity, some positive and some negative. Electricity has the property of like charges repelling and opposite charges attracting. Rubbing a glass rod with silk or an ebonite rod with flannel can generate electricity and attract light objects such as paper scraps and dust (Figure 1). After rubbing an ebonite rod to generate negative electricity and suspending it in the air with silk thread, and then rubbing a glass rod to generate positive electricity and bringing it close to the ebonite rod, they will attract each other (Figure 2). However, if there were two ebonite rods or two glass rods, this would not be possible. When clouds in the sky containing opposite charges approach each other in mid-air, they will attract each other, but air does not easily conduct electricity, so there must be extremely high electrical pressure for the current to pass through the air. When it first passes through the air, countless electric sparks occur (Figure 3), and at the same time, the air is broken down by the electricity and rapidly vibrates into a loud noise. This light is called lightning, and the sound is thunder. Like the whirligig we play with (Figure 4), the faster it is pulled, the more violently the bamboo board vibrates the air, and the sound gradually becomes louder. The formation of thunder is the same. However, light travels fast, at a speed of about 300 million meters per second, while sound travels slowly, at only 331 meters per second. Therefore, although sound and light occur simultaneously in mid-air, we see the lightning first and then hear the thunder when they reach us.

Since Benjamin Franklin (Figure 5) discovered electricity in clouds more than 180 years ago, the principle of thunder and lightning has been proven very thoroughly. Currently, many European and American power laboratories even have people experimenting with artificial lightning! The so-called thunder striking people is actually an accidental association of electrocution. This radiating electricity, whether it is a person or an animal, is fatal upon contact, and houses and large trees are often burned down by electrocution. Therefore, tall buildings now have lightning rods to attract opposite charges to the ground (Figure 6). During thunderstorms, do not walk outside, do not wear wet clothes, and do not lean against high walls or large trees to avoid electrocution.

The Benefits and Harms of Eating Watermelon 262

— Bing Yu

In modern nutrition science, how much value does watermelon, the king of summer fruits, have? According to the research results of the famous medical scientist Dr. Xue Tai, the flesh contains 95.96% water, 2.87% carbohydrates, 0.78% protein, 0.20% ash, 0.10% fat, and 0.09% fiber. However, when we eat watermelon, for example, red-fleshed watermelon, after eating all the red part, the white part is discarded because it tastes bland. However, the composition of the white discarded part is not much different from the red part, except that the ash content is slightly less, and the protein and fat are more than the white part. Also, the sugar content of watermelon is 6 to 8%, two-thirds of which is fructose. Compared to the central part without seeds, the surrounding part with more seeds, and the inner skin part without the outer skin, the central part contains the most fructose, glucose, and sucrose, the surrounding part is second, and the part near the outer skin is the least, so the thickness of the sweetness varies layer by layer. As for the vitamins contained in watermelon, they are the most abundant among summer fruits, so people with chronic kidney disease benefit from eating more watermelon, which has a special diuretic effect. This year's climate is unusually hot, and the sales of soda, cold drinks, refreshing beverages, and fruits are very large, indicating that many people in society are eating them. However, indulging in temporary gratification and eating too much watermelon will cause abdominal distension, and various diseases will follow, because watermelon is a plant that is not easily digested, and it contains too much water, which is harmful to the stomach, intestines, and kidneys. (Editor's note): Children, when eating watermelon, do not swallow the seeds. Chew the pulp and spit it out immediately, so there will be no harm from indigestion.

Standing an Egg Upright 263

— Wang Qianchuo

Little friends! Can you stand a raw egg (duck egg is also acceptable) upright on the table without damaging it? Or do you even think it is impossible? In fact, it is not difficult. Just hold the egg in your hand and shake it gently a few times, then slowly stand it upright on a smooth table, and it will stand up.

There are a few points to pay attention to when doing this game: (1) The movement must be steady and not hasty; (2) It must be stood on a smooth table; (3) If it cannot stand upright immediately, shake the egg a few more times.

Finally, I want to tell you the reason why the egg stands upright: Before the egg is shaken, its entire weight is concentrated in the center of the egg, so it can lie horizontally on the table. After the egg is shaken, its entire weight gradually gathers at one end of the egg. We stand this end upright on the table, and of course it can stand up.

Blue Fish and White Fish 264

— Da Zhai

In the water, the blue fish always has many white fish following it closely, why are they so close? Because the white fish are greedy and want to take advantage of free food, the blue fish often cannot eat the food it finds.

However, children may have questions about this. The blue fish forages for food, and the white fish also forages for food. Why do the white fish want to steal the food the blue fish finds? The blue fish has already found food in its mouth, why doesn't it eat it itself, but instead it is stolen by the white fish? Isn't this very special?

Originally, the blue fish has sharp teeth in its throat and chews food very well. It likes to eat snails the most, chewing the snails in its throat and then spitting them out, causing the fine hard shells to sink, and then eating the clean meat. Who knew that the white fish would take this opportunity to take advantage of it. When the snail meat was rippling in the water, they would swarm up and搶吃it. The food that the blue fish was about to eat was enjoyed by the white fish who ate for free. The white fish simply had no teeth and could neither eat the whole snail nor taste the delicious snail meat, and always wanted to take the opportunity to steal it, so they always followed the blue fish closely.

One day, an old fisherman was fishing under the shade of a willow tree on the堤岸, his eyes fixed on the mark on the fishing line. As long as the mark moved, he would know that a fish was hooked, and he would immediately lift it up. The blue fish and white fish happened to swim to the fishing hook. The fishing hook was baited with earthworm meat. The white fish followed the old pattern of抢螺蛳meat, hurriedly抢着 it. As soon as it reached its mouth, the line was lifted up, and with a flip, it was already in the old fisherman's fish basket. The old fisherman put down the fishing hook again and caught white fish again. This happened several times. The blue fish could not grab the bait and was never hooked, so it swayed and swam to another place. The white fish were still struggling in the fish basket. The old fisherman smiled and said to the white fish, "You have always loved to take advantage of small gains. You must know that greed for small gains will eventually suffer great losses. Do you realize it now? But regret is useless."

Children, people's behavior should be upright and honest, and value integrity and self-respect. Do not贪图 those improper advantages that are not rightfully yours.贪图 Small gains often lead to great disasters.

Small Craft

Hand-Cranked Fan 265

— Yong Cai

Little friends! Do you think the weather is hot this year? I will teach you how to make a small toy to cool off the summer heat! However, before you start making this small toy, you must first prepare some simple materials: a piece of wood 8 inches long and 5 inches wide, two empty cigarette cans, four bamboo sticks 6 inches long and 3/4 inches thick and wide, 15 inches of thick lead wire, and a section of iron pipe 1.5 inches long (this section of iron pipe is an important material in this small toy, and its thickness should be slightly thicker than the prepared thick lead wire. If you don't know how to make it, you can go to an iron shop to make one, three or four copper coins will be enough.) A strip of flat, wide tape, 丨丨After the above materials are prepared, we can start making it.

When starting to make this toy, we can divide it into two steps: the first step is to make the wings, and the second step is to make the axle.

First step: First cut open the empty cigarette cans, according to the pattern and size in (Figure 1) 丨丨密达尺丨, cut out two identical wings, then cut a piece of iron skin the size of a copper coin from the remaining iron. After cutting, first cross the two wings at the center, make a hole in the center point of the wings with a nail, and then install it on one end of the iron pipe, making sure it is tightly attached and does not move (it is best to ask the ironmonger to solder it firmly). On the other end of the iron pipe, make a hole in the same way with the round iron piece, and install it tightly as shown in Figure 1. After installing, cut a section of thick lead wire 2.5 inches long and insert it into the inside of the iron pipe (note: the iron pipe should be free to move on the lead wire). Then take the prepared bamboo material, drill a hole in the upper end of two of the sticks, and tightly attach both ends of the lead wire to the holes, as shown in Figure 3. In this way, the first step is completed.

Second step: Take the lids of the two cigarette cans and close them tightly together. Then make a hole in the center of the lids, insert the remaining lead wire tightly, and also make sure it does not move (it is best to also ask the ironmonger to solder it firmly), as shown in Figure 4. After inserting, drill two holes in the upper end of the remaining two bamboo sticks in the same way. These two holes should be drilled a little larger so that the lead wire has room to move in the middle. After drilling, insert the lead wire separately, and after inserting, bend the lead wire into a handle, as shown in Figure 5. In this way, the second step is also completed.

After both steps are done, take the four bamboo sticks and钉在them on the wooden board according to the appropriate position and distance. Then take the flat, wide tape and tie it to the iron pipe and axle, as shown in Figure 6. In this way, the entire project is completed.

How to play: Whenever you are reviewing your homework or have nothing to do, put it next to you and gently搖動the axle. The four wings will quickly轉動, and at the same time, the cool and large wind will襲面的來驅逐the summer heat around you. Little friends! You see how interesting and practical this toy is.

— Xuan

These days, women seem particularly disappointing. In this time of national crisis and impending home collapse, instead of coming out to do things beneficial to society, they like to be foreign slaves, salespeople for foreign goods, and take this opportunity to dress in a妖妖艶艶manner to seduce the opposite sex.
