The Problem of Higher Education 267

— Ying

Now is the time when countless school recruitment advertisements occupy the prominent positions of various newspapers; it is also the time when young men and women students徘徊奔波, looking for a way to higher education. On the other hand, the establishment of the "Beiping University Graduates' Vocational Movement Alliance" has resonated throughout the country, which fully proves that students have no way out. In this current society where "more students graduate from schools, the more unemployed members society increases," female students are particularly unemployed. Because in this male-centered society, the scope of women's occupations is very narrow, not to mention in this large reserve army of unemployment, women lack experience in争夺饭碗, and are also treated differently by society, so finding a job is naturally more difficult than climbing to the sky. Therefore, now that the lucky female students are able to仰承祖泽, and can go to higher education, in order to find a preparation for future outlets, they have to pay more attention to this serious problem.

I think there are at least two points that female youths who are going to higher education should carefully consider: one is the school; the other is the subject.

The choice of school is the first and main task for those who are going to higher education. However, the method of selection cannot solely rely on the advertisements and regulations published in the newspaper, because now, some schools have already been commercialized, and their regulations and advertisements inevitably have the deceptive nature of buying and selling. The advertisement says that someone is the principal and someone is the chairman of the board, nothing more than holding名人 to do招摇撞骗of a cover. Therefore, we had better inquire from reliable friends and classmates to get the真相. The criteria for choosing a school should pay attention to: (1) whether the school is public or private. If it is private, then how is its fund? How about the equipment? And how about the teachers? Should be considered, according to what we know, the tuition fees of public and private schools are often inversely proportional, and the tuition fees of public schools with sufficient funds must be low, and the equipment must be excellent, because it is not supported by the tuition fees of students. On the contrary,不三不四的"wild chicken" schools (large, middle, and small schools are the same), most of them do not have reliable funds, and all teachers' salaries, rent, equipment, and all other expenses are "wool from the sheep - from the students that裏" squeeze out, therefore the tuition fees of private schools are very high, and they have to be high. At the same time, most of these schools are for the purpose of business, and will not hire excellent teachers with high salaries. (2) What should be noted is the reputation of the school in the society, and the general level of knowledge of the school graduates, which is also very important, because schools with good reputation are respected by the society, and students with good grades are needed by the society. (3) What should be noted is which subject of the school has the best equipment, and whether it is close to the旨趣 of the person, because a suitable environment can arouse one's interest in learning, so that the effect of "doing more with less" can be achieved. (4) Girls should choose schools with male and female classmates, because in this way, they can cultivate social, open, equal and respectful habits, and also increase the psychology of competition in learning between men and women, unlike some women's "special schools," which spend all their precious time learning cooking, sewing, embroidery, and other courses, and neglect the cultivation of basic knowledge of natural science or social science.

As for the choice of subjects, I think we should choose the important ones from the subjects we like and learn them, and also take into account the needs of the society, which leads to social problems.

Everyone knows that social problems have the closest relationship with us. Some people who study natural science often ignore this social problem. But everyone knows that these natural sciences 丨 physics, chemistry, mathematics, astronomy, are related to social sciences, and at the same time, her application needs a social environment, as for social sciences 丨 such as economics is the basis of society, and literature, education, law, philosophy, politics... are the upper construction of social organization. If we want to make what we have learned in line with reality; to correctly understand society; to solve the difficulties of society, and to achieve our expectations for society, we must make a determination to do in-depth research when going to higher education.

Finally, let us talk about the "good wife and loving mother" education that some people have recently advocated that women should return to the family. I don't know if these people are afraid that the increase in female生力军 in occupational competition, so they want to drive women home裏, to live the life of a cook and a female worker, so that everything in society is独裁by men. If this is the case, not only will it not solve the basic contradictions of the current society, but it will deepen it more and more. This is undoubtedly a counter-era倒车 method, which is no different from the foolish actions of workers打毁machines in the early eighteenth century. In fact, if women only seek some "good wife and loving mother" education, and go home裏 to "serve her husband and follow her son," according to the general situation of the current society, it will only increase the burden on men, and cut off the road to women's economic independence, which is only suitable for a few "闻人"’s grandmothers and wives. Regarding these, we have explained it very clearly in the previous text that marrying is not a woman's career. Moreover, the number of women who can go to higher education and find a job is very small. It is impossible to make up for the current large-scale unemployed Chinese society with this "鳳毛麟角"’s微而又微 number. At the same time, we are determined not to live a parasitic, inhuman life of shackles. Our "贤良" should be placed in all undertakings that are beneficial to society. This is also a problem that students who are preparing to go to higher education should pay attention to.

Words from a Female Teacher 268

— Bi Wu

After reading "Divorce and Educational Bankruptcy"

In today's era when everything is not on the right track, the life of a female teacher is of course often unreasonable. First, in terms of sex, until now, except for a very small number of enlightened people, it is still believed that female teachers should maintain the life of a holy woman, just like傳道師姑. Marriage (referring to marriage that is not arranged by parents and媒奺’s words) has been regarded as亵渎, and divorce is even more悖谬; as recorded in the previous issue of this journal "Divorce and Educational Bankruptcy," the city of H actually had such an absurd statement about Ms. C. Educational bankruptcy and divorce do have some indirect relationship; but one person's divorce due to disagreement is educational bankruptcy. This is as illogical as "the river water falls a thousand feet" and "a cliff is ten thousand feet deep."

How can education go bankrupt? Many people attribute it to the educators' "moral depravity and loss of integrity"; but educators are not all selected unscrupulous people, this explanation is always too唯心. As for female teachers' marriage and divorce, and even being regarded as an element of educational bankruptcy, this is even more of a superficial understanding of Freud's theory.

Ideally, even if educators cannot be great personalities or creators of great culture, they should also be the搬运者 of these two. But in reality, everyone is like a day laborer,搬运ing to the next generation of people, are fragmented bricks and tiles,停了機械, and even污穢糞土! Life and the system force him to do so; if Pestalozzi were resurrected, he would not be able to save the entire destruction here.

However, it is irresponsible to attribute everything to the environment. Soundness itself can be half of the effort. The ignorance, shallow views, narrowness, and hypocrisy of general educators... do not necessarily depend on the environment for improvement: and these automatic improvements may have more needs in the area of female teachers. Generally speaking, because women have been雌伏 for thousands of years, once they reach the equal position of teachers with men, they will be complacent and unwilling to seek more. For learning and knowledge, the day of graduation from母校 is the absolute graduation; for social and life problems, they inherit the spirit of雌伏 and think that it is not essential. What supports and excites them daily is the self-comfort and self-aggrandizement of "outstanding from the crowd"; in many places, there must be a装作 of loneliness. The reasons for the popular singleism some time ago are complicated, but this装作 is the main angle. Its influence, combined with the feudal concept of貞操, has further consolidated the social requirement for female teachers to be圣女. As a result, our students cannot see a trace of the尾巴骨 of personality influence from female teachers, but only see the皮毛 of hypocrisy.

Some装作 for a lifetime, but some inevitably变节 later. But her shallow and narrow knowledge cannot make her understand that this is the nature of humanity, and to come out with光明坦白; for ordinary people, especially for students, she can only come out with an increased degree of hypocrisy. A唯美 old friend of mine often said angrily: "It's better to be a prostitute than to be a female teacher!" How cruel prostitutes are, she doesn't seem to know: the boredom of female teachers' lives, she knows thoroughly.

The divorce incident of Ms. C in city H can only be used as a material for field research when teaching the problem of love and marriage: if it is believed that sexual life should be avoided from students, and the situation of educational bankruptcy caused by the environment and each other is not given in-depth research and reflection, but lightly推 in a certain person's certain matter, this is a丢人 statement in the male and female education circles.

However, depending on the situation, my colleagues in the female education community, whether they can break the false, self-enclosed life: whether they can do more to exert a little effort on the influence of personality and the搬运 of culture, but it should have a stronger self-criticism.

Re-reading "Nora" 269

— First

Hot, hot, truly an extraordinary heat! Heat that breaks sixty years of records, a heat that we who have only lived thirty years have never experienced. Don't you feel your head spinning? Don't you feel your body weary? If you haven't tasted this, you can't know how difficult heat is to bear. If you have tasted how difficult this heat is to bear, you will be afraid when you think of it.

I deeply believe that the truth in this world can only be truly understood through experience. Theories, no matter how novel and profound they are, if they do not come from personal experience, are inevitably just fantasies, unreliable. I certainly won't believe them. Conversely, if it is the truth, it will make you believe. Otherwise, it just means you are too naive to be able to experience it.

During the scorching summer vacation, the hot wind makes people listless, and nothing can lift their spirits. But you can't just sit idle and let this long summer pass. So, reading novels became the only way to relieve the summer heat. These past two days, I have been reading Pan Jiaxun's translation of the Ibsen collection. I had read this book when it was first published more than ten years ago. At that time, I was a seventeen- or eighteen-year-old girl, newly liberated in thought from a closed-off environment. Seeing a member of the opposite sex, I would always lower my head in shyness; how could I have the courage to think about the relationship between the sexes at all? Moreover, at that time, public social interactions between the sexes were just beginning, and everything had to be done cautiously to avoid giving people something to gossip about. After all, I was a product of the restraints of traditional ethics, and I naturally tended towards the sublime of "spiritualism." I treated both sexes as "people," and letters written to female friends were love letters, and letters written to male friends were also love letters. I never thought that different things could happen between men and women.

Under these circumstances, I read Ibsen's "Nora," "Ghosts," and "The Lady from the Sea," and I treated them as plays, as stories. Although I understood a little bit of the abstract concept—knew that women should not be men's playthings, relying on men to live; but later I became a man's plaything and relied on a man to live without even realizing it. As for things like sexual life, sexual hygiene, and sexual diseases, even when I gave birth to my third child, I still hadn't fully understood them. It wasn't until an accidental stroke of luck—yes, I can say that was my luck—that liberated me from the hands of my "husband," and only now do I truly sympathize with Nora, Alida, and Mrs. Alving; only now do I truly understand, "First and foremost, I am a human being. Just like you. —No matter what, I must strive to be a human being." "Complete freedom! Still, take responsibility! Don't take responsibility! With this, everything will be different."

How has the environment abused me! How has life tormented me! I painfully struggled forward in the deep ditch of hardship. However, I am completely free, I take responsibility myself—take on the responsibility of being a human being. I feel that I am a person, striving to be a person, and there is an indescribable joy in my heart! Thinking back to the past, living in a dream of love, being a wife in her husband's hands, even my clothing and food were managed by him. He said I was stupid and ugly, not letting me take full responsibility for the family, not giving me control over the family finances; buying some decorations without my consent, telling me to dress up beautifully and look good according to his wishes. And his sexual organs became diseased because of his excessive masturbation, but he didn't tell me clearly—I deeply believe he understood. His sexual life was selfish and self-serving. He didn't pay attention to hygiene, and didn't sincerely practice restraint. He was an extravagant, unrestrained person.

Believing in "Love is supreme" and "Love is unconditional"—these words that men use to deceive women—subject to the criticism of justice, the condemnation of conscience, is so shameful! Alas! Even now, when I think back to it, I'm still afraid! Still trembling! Just like the record-breaking heat of sixty years that killed so many people, and I almost, didn't die from the heat, it's just as terrifying.

Dear friend, have you, like me, tasted the life of a Nora, an Alida, or a Mrs. Alving, or other various and different slaves, inhuman lives? Do you also want to taste the flavor of "striving to be a free person, taking on the responsibilities of a person," a refreshing way to relieve the summer heat? This is a bitter medicine, which will give you temporary pain. But it will remove your disease, and when you wake up, you will feel comfortable and happy! That taste, like eating bitter melon, eating olives, in the bitterness, in the astringency, there is a subtle and indescribable deliciousness.

Letter 270

This is a personal letter from my old friend Bai Wei, mostly criticisms and suggestions for this publication, so I am publishing it for readers to see.

Editor

Zi Jiu:

Because I wanted to have a deep talk with you, I tried to see you dozens of times. I paid a visit to your residence a month ago, but you weren't home. I wanted to visit again, but it was delayed.

You are a capable fellow, working tirelessly on many things. Compared to you, I, this useless thing, feel ashamed to death! So you, being clever, knew this early on and cut off our friendship long ago.

When Ding Ling flew to the sky, I was rolling around in hell, gasping for breath; when you were rising step by step, working hard, even though I had crawled out of the gates of hell, I couldn't crawl anymore. Currently, I am suffering from pain that cuts like a knife and burns like fire. You and I are truly "heaven and earth," like not being able to touch the blue sky, I can't reach you. Recalling the years when we were classmates and lived together, I bought you fresh flowers, set up painting scenes for you, accompanied you in painting from morning till night, spent the whole day with you wandering the snowy scenery of Inokashira Park, and finally, I persuaded you to watch operas… Those, are all like "flowing water, falling flowers, spring has gone." Only the youthful, passionate friendship of that time, and your momentary beauty, often stir up waves in my memories, making my internal organs feel sore and distressed.

During the ten years of separation, although I went to see you several times, met you several times, you were openly cold towards me, as if you and I had never had a friendship.

Zi Jiu, is that my hypersensitivity? Or does the environment determine that you and I can only be like that? (Omission)

This spring, in the cultural education hall's living room, you brought up the news of the slander against me in the Morning Post and laughed at me, as if it were very serious, as if I were immersed in happiness.

It's no wonder you, who knows my personality? Who can prove my real life? If someone knew my personality, understood my steadfast, painful real life, no matter who, even if they wouldn't shed tears for me, they would feel a sad and mournful emotion. (Omission)

Let me tell you: for more than ten years, ever since you all knew about my sensational romance until today, I haven't enjoyed even half a month of life's pleasures, only a miserable life more profound than any tragedy, biting me relentlessly.

Enough with the nonsense, let's get down to business.

Why do I want to say all this nonsense to you? I want to lift the heavy curtain separating us, open my heart, and talk to you about serious matters.

A few days ago, you said to me, "The reason I accepted editing the Women's Garden is to give us a place to speak." In this era where passionate blood can only subside, where women must return to the family, you took on this editorship to give us a place to speak, you are right!

But, what has been said in your garden in the past? What do you want to say in the future? What is your overall plan? Just gossiping about women's common knowledge? Having scholarly gentlemen come up with profound studies? Standing in a detached position, blandly discussing women's issues? Friend, don't leave this sharp society, don't leave these sharp women, you are just like a storyteller in the streets, telling old stories!

True, people like Bi Yun, Bi Wu, and Bi Yao have also repeatedly made many famous speeches scolding the bad customs of the past.

However, new evil winds, corruption, decadence, such as their worship of money, their bloodsucking, their cunning, their ruthlessness; their demon-like appearance, their fox-like intentions; their failure to improve themselves, their living from day to day, their gladly being soulless meat puppets; their vanity, their laziness, seeking only material satisfaction, willingly submitting to wicked men for life; their lack of self-respect, their willful abandon, their dizzying, confused relationships with countless members of the opposite sex, living a degenerate, promiscuous life… Have any of you come out to criticize and discuss these sharp phenomena of the present?

On the bustling streets, the streets are full of clothes racks made of foreign materials, lips painted as red as a vampire, flaunting their bloodsucking hearts; in theaters or playgrounds, they are filled with soulless pieces of flesh, their vile giggling making people nauseous, their frantic swaying making people cringe, walking like wandering corpses, extravagant to the extreme; in large family mansions, there are mostly modern women who are preoccupied with dressing up and beautifying themselves, who are idle and wasteful, they neither know their responsibilities to the nation and society, nor do they take care of their families and children, only mahjong and movies can while away their time, Peking opera, dancing, and affairs are also indispensable stimuli for them. Have you ever loudly called out to these bloodsucking, parasitic women, telling them to quickly get up and be human beings, or else, like killing mosquitoes and flies, will you implement measures to drive them away?

Most of the women in Chinese cities are bustling, lazy, and shameless, not living as human beings there. How many make people want to frown and feel nauseous, ah, women are demons! (To be continued)

Snippets of a Female Worker's Life 271

— Wen Juan

Today marks exactly one year since I came to this factory. It is said that from today onwards, night shifts will begin. My uncle came to call me, telling me to go eat dinner immediately. I must be at the factory by 5:30 to work the night shift. So, I dropped what I was washing and went to eat.

Tonight is a bit too much to handle. Not having worked the night shift for several months, now that it's starting again, my head feels a bit dizzy. What I hate most is the four-month-old baby in my belly, causing trouble there, sliding up and down, moving non-stop. There's no stool to sit on, standing next to the machine for a full twelve hours like this, how can I endure it!

Sister Zhang saw that I was uncomfortable and told me to take a day off first. But I still勉强 to support myself, gritting my teeth and working on.

Alas, it's really too much to handle! The machine is malfunctioning, malfunctioning, again and again. By the time I had just connected the broken warp ends, the shuttle in front had punched a hole in the Indian silk, tearing out more than an inch, and then reconnected twenty or thirty ends. With such constant ups and downs, the baby moved too uncomfortably, my waist ached, and my legs felt like two sticks, already without sensation. I really, really wanted a bed to lie down comfortably for a while, just for a moment would be enough.

It's two o'clock now, I turned off the machine, wanting to doze off next to it. Just as my eyes were closing, suddenly, "Wham…" I woke up with a start, only to find that the machine on the opposite side, machine number two, probably dozing off herself, let out such a loud scream to excite her spirit, but I really couldn't support it anymore, my head felt like it was splitting open. The slow, clumsy "tat-tat-tat" of the motor sound echoed mechanically in my brain forever. My heart was working as frantically as a shuttle in my chest at extreme speed, it almost wanted to jump out of my mouth. Then, I vomited, vomited all over the floor. My uncle asked for a day off for me, telling me to go home to recuperate immediately.扶 to the factory gate, he went inside. He seemed to be grumbling: "Miss is used to being pampered!" Alas, men really don't understand women's suffering, even my own uncle is like this. If I had the strength at that moment, I would definitely have turned around and scolded him. On the way home, I vomited three more times in a row, it was so hard.

Back home, I was already like a dying person, but all kinds of thoughts surged up in my mind together: If I continue to be sick like this forever, can I continue my work tomorrow? If I don't go to the factory, how will my livelihood be solved? I can't even maintain the most basic living standard now, how can I bear this double burden when the child is born in the future? My heart is broken! My head is spinning! Tears are falling like a spring! Oh God! Tragic fate!

Abstract of Laws and Regulations 272

Section 3: General Effects of Marriage

Article 1000: A wife uses her own surname preceded by her husband's surname, a live-in son-in-law uses his own surname preceded by his wife's surname. However, this does not apply if the parties have otherwise agreed.

Article 1001: Husband and wife have a mutual obligation to cohabit, but this does not apply if there is a legitimate reason for not being able to cohabit.

Article 1002: A wife's residence is the husband's residence, a live-in son-in-law's residence is the wife's residence.

Article 1003: Husband and wife are mutual agents for daily household affairs. If one party abuses the aforementioned agency power, the other party may restrict it, but it may not be used to oppose a third party acting in good faith.

Section 4: Marital Property System

Subsection 1: General Principles

Article 1004: Husband and wife may, before or after marriage, choose through contract one of the property systems stipulated in this law as their marital property system.

Article 1005: If husband and wife have not established a marital property system by contract, the statutory property system shall be their marital property system unless otherwise provided by law.

Article 1006: The establishment, modification, or termination of a marital property system contract requires the consent of the legal guardian if the parties are minors or persons under interdiction.

Article 1007: The establishment, modification, or termination of a marital property system contract shall be in writing.

Article 1008: The establishment, modification, or termination of a marital property system contract may not be used to oppose third parties unless it has been registered.

Article 1009: If one party of a husband and wife is declared bankrupt, their marital property system shall naturally become a separate property system.

Article 1010: Under one of the following circumstances, the court shall declare the change to a separate property system upon the request of one party of the husband and wife:

1. When one party of the husband and wife is required by law to pay household living expenses but does not pay.

2. When the property of the husband or wife is insufficient to pay off their debts, or when the total property of the husband and wife is insufficient to pay off the total debt.

3. When one party of the husband and wife is required by law to obtain the consent of the other party for the disposal of property, and the other party refuses to consent without just cause.

Article 1011: If a creditor has attached the property of one party of a husband and wife without receiving repayment, the court may declare the change to a separate property system upon the application of the creditor.

Article 1012: Husband and wife may, during the continuation of the marital relationship, terminate their property contract or change to another type of agreed property system by contract.

Article 1013: The following properties are separate properties:

1. Items exclusively for the personal use of the husband or wife.

2. Items necessary for the profession of the husband or wife.

3. Gifts received by the husband or wife, with the donor stating that they are separate properties.

4. Compensation earned by the wife through labor.

Article 1014: Husband and wife may stipulate by contract that certain properties are separate properties.

Article 1015: The provisions regarding separate property shall apply to the separate properties stipulated in the preceding two articles.

Article 1016: Properties belonging to the husband and wife at the time of marriage and properties acquired by the husband and wife during the continuation of the marital relationship are their joint properties. However, the wife's separate property as stipulated in Article 1013 is not included.

Increased Grain Margin Has Had a Restrictive Effect

Flour Futures Gradually Return to Normal 286

Flour Margin to be Changed to $500 Starting Next Week

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the markets for each month showed a trend of first falling and then stabilizing. Buyers and sellers were mostly watching and waiting. Factories released slightly, while customers entered slightly. The situation had entered a stable phase. Since the exchange gradually increased the margin for outside speculators (from 250 yuan to 750 yuan), those without the strength had no choice but to wait and see. This has also had a great impact on the recent stabilization of the market. As a result, the current month remained unchanged, September improved by 0.015 yuan, October improved by 0.0075 yuan, November improved by 0.02 yuan, and December and January improved by 0.015 yuan. Starting next week, the flour exchange will change the margin for both buyers and sellers to 500 yuan. In the future, if the market becomes more stable, it will be restored to its original state. It is reported that the market has been announced.

| Grain Exchange Brokers Propose Reducing Margin |

Yesterday in the wheat futures market, after the opening in the morning, the markets for each month showed a situation of near-term weakness and far-term stability. This situation is also due to the increase in the margin, which has invisibly restricted speculative activities. As a result, August fell by 0.06 yuan, September fell by 0.08 yuan, October fell by 0.06 yuan, November fell by 0.02 yuan, and December fell by 0.05 yuan. Large wheat mills unanimously held firm, and the market did not open for trading. Brokers at the miscellaneous grains exchange have reportedly made a proposal to the exchange authorities regarding the margin because the market is gradually stabilizing. If the wheat market is within 0.2 yuan, the margin will still be changed to 280 yuan. If it is outside of 0.2 yuan, it will be changed to 400 yuan. The soybean oil margin is proposed to be changed to 210 yuan. However, it will only be determined next week whether the exchange will allow it.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Amateur Musings

Labor and Interest 293

— Anfu

When we are born into this world crying, Heaven endows us with five senses and four limbs. This is sufficient proof that we humans are not born into this world to enjoy leisure, but to labor. Since our human duty is to labor, then we should recognize the goals of labor, discern right from wrong, and good from evil. We must use all the strength of our lives, without discouragement or interruption, and strive forward. Only in this way will we have a day of success! However, the facts tell us that humans are animals with life and emotions, so the environment and personality, etc., all have a considerable relationship with humans. Therefore, when we engage in a certain kind of labor for a long time, we often develop a kind of aversion and produce a feeling of dislike for the occupation or a state of mind disliking it. The growth of this kind of mentality or state is most likely to hinder the progress of labor invisibly, resulting in a decrease in productivity. Moreover, this will not only make the employer who hires you feel that your ability to handle affairs has declined, but from your own point of view, you will also feel boredom and pain.

What medicine can cure or eliminate this dangerous disease? In fact, the occurrence of this disease can simply be said to have no medicine to cure it; if there is one, it is interest. Carlyle said, "We most welcome those who sing while working." Xu Mi also said, "Ordinary people who hold optimism about anything in the world are better than those who have a thousand gold income every year." The so-called singing person and optimistic person here are actually people who are full of interest in their hearts when they work! Here, we can also randomly cite a person as a representative, such as Smith (Sydney Smith 1770-1845). He was a British pastor and also a famous writer. But how did he succeed? We can see in his letter to his daughter: "The position I am in now was not what I originally chose, but since I have engaged in it, then I can also feel at ease and like it; because this is much more manly than those who think highly of themselves and want to dislike their occupation." This kind of lack of a fixed standard for choosing a career is not an appropriate thing; however, being able to generate interest in labor is indeed something worthy of our emulation. At the same time, he liked to say throughout his life: "Let us glorify the room." His meaning is that people should abandon darkness and let in sunlight; that is to say, in the labor of life, one should try to abandon the boring and tasteless page, and should try to promote the interesting side of labor. From this point of view, the reason why Smith was able to succeed and enjoy fame was also produced by the harmony of labor and interest.

Looking at everything in China today, whether it is the country, society, or individual life, a phenomenon of economic depression can be seen almost everywhere. However, if everyone can follow their duties, not sigh, not frown, and work hard without negativity, as if using sweat to restrain us, and at the same time try to find interest in labor as the driving force for our struggle, then in less than ten years, I believe that everything at that time must be stronger than it is now. You only need to look at Japan as a good example for our country, and Smith and Edison are good role models for us as human beings.

In short, life should be about laboring, and it is an inevitable trend to feel bored and dull with labor; however, it depends on whether you can find interest in the boring and dull life as a stimulant. Because only the interest gained from boredom is true interest. It will continue forever, as long as your life; and its benefits to us humans cannot be described in words or writing.

Life

Film Critic 294

— Liren

Although film criticism has long been popular in Europe and the United States, it must be said that its awakening and widespread attention in China only occurred after the January 28th Incident. After the January 28th Incident, Chinese films have made considerable progress, which is visible to everyone. This is mostly thanks to the "gifts" of the Japanese imperialist cannons; however, the efforts of film critics in helping the growth of new Chinese films should not be ignored. Film criticism was originally a record of audience opinions; filmmakers who take profit-making as their sole purpose naturally dare not ignore this valuable opinion and go down a dead end. Today, the films of talented scholars and beautiful ladies, and the martial arts films with flying swords, have been spurned by a vast audience; the mission of film has been recognized as a weapon to fight for the freedom and liberation of the broad masses and the nation, rather than a pastime exclusively for those who have leisure. This recognition of the great function of film is undoubtedly promoted by the efforts of film critics.

Because film criticism is valued and welcomed by the broad audience, newspapers, in order to compete for their readers, have had to compete to publish film journals and carry film reviews; as a result, some people with artistic cultivation and film knowledge have appeared and been valued as "film critics." Here, I want to go on to briefly describe their lifestyle.

First, I want to mention the "remuneration" they can obtain from the newspaper. Generally, newspapers have two methods of paying film critics: by word count and by article. If calculated by word count, the remuneration per thousand words can be roughly divided into six levels, namely, five yuan, four yuan, three yuan, two yuan, one and a half yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. It cannot be said that the difference between these numbers is quite large. The reason for this is mostly due to the difference in the newspaper's film advertising revenue and its economic capacity; a small part, however, is that some newspapers have different methods of paying special contributors with higher status and ordinary contributors. For example, a certain newspaper pays three yuan per thousand words for special film contributions, while only one yuan and fifty cents per thousand words for ordinary film contributions. Larger newspapers generally pay no less than five to four yuan per thousand words to special film critics with status; ordinary film critics are paid only three yuan and two yuan per thousand words. (The above refers to different newspapers.) Smaller newspapers probably pay a maximum of three yuan per thousand words to special film critics; it is also very common to pay two yuan or one and a half yuan per thousand words, and it is not entirely non-existent to pay only one yuan per thousand words.

If calculated by the article (this refers specifically to "film reviews" of a certain film), the highest price a film critic can get for racking their brains after watching a film is probably only three yuan, and the least will not

Page 20

be less than two yuan. Some are paid two yuan and fifty cents per article. In addition, since the minimum prices of the top theaters in this city are one yuan, six jiao, and five jiao respectively, the newspaper generally pays a few jiao more to film critics who spend more money on watching movies.

Regardless of whether the remuneration is calculated by word count or by article, the cost of watching movies is generally borne by the film critics themselves. However, artists have always been poor friends, and unfortunately, film critics are no exception. When they cannot afford it themselves, they may have to pre-pay some movie money from the newspaper or the person in charge, or even pre-pay some manuscript fees. But this situation is very rare and uncommon.

Now I want to talk about the possible monthly income of an average film critic. This depends on the amount of remuneration and whether they have enough time to write. It is not entirely a fantasy to earn as much as two hundred yuan per month if one gets high remuneration and writes a lot; one hundred and several tens of yuan is not entirely impossible for such people. We know that in addition to writing "film reviews," film critics also have to write film essays, miscellaneous feelings, reviews, and other film review texts, as well as play reviews in related art theater, and sometimes even write poems, novels, and sketches to occupy a place in journals and newspapers to share a part of the manuscript fees. By piecing together all kinds of income, the result of their racking their brains can sometimes be quite considerable. But such people are a very small minority. Most people earn only thirty or forty yuan per month, and some can only earn ten or twenty yuan per month. This is mostly because they produce little and receive low remuneration.

Regarding "film reviews," I would like to say a few more words. Generally, newspapers have fixed and non-fixed arrangements for the theaters where film critics watch movies. Some are assigned to watch a certain theater exclusively, and some are decided on a temporary basis and notified to each film critic by telephone. As for the number of film critics in each newspaper, I would also like to mention it. Generally, the number of special film critics in each newspaper is usually no more than three to five people, and there are not many more than that, although it does not seem to be the case.

Now I want to go on to talk about the origins of these film critics. Most of them are people in the film industry, the drama industry, and the literary world, and occasionally a few members of the civilized drama faction and the mandarin duck butterfly faction are also involved. Some practitioners in the film industry who have insufficient income or even unemployment are very eager to find their way out from the field of film criticism; sometimes there are also some publicists employed by certain production companies and related people who come out to write wonderful articles that boast about themselves. These critics in the drama and literary circles, because most of them have a deeper literary cultivation and richer life experience, although they may not be 100% experts in film, their understanding of film art and their enthusiastic research, as an appreciative critic, their valuable opinions contributed to the new Chinese film and the audience are well worth noting. As for those backward film critics of the civilized drama faction and the mandarin duck butterfly faction who specialize in praising thighs and breasts and other erotic scenes and who take low-level interests as the first meaning, they have long declined with the decline of the love films of talented scholars and beautiful ladies and the martial arts films with flying swords, and have long been forgotten by the vast and progressive audience. For example, in the recent debate between soft theorists and film realists, they lost the sympathy of the audience and did not gain people's favor.

Writing to this point, I would like to mention some new ways out for some film critics. Writing film reviews is ultimately a very hard work. If there are better jobs to do, some film critics will lower their status and sell their knowledge. They may be recruited by a film company, and in exchange for remuneration, they can manipulate film reviews and create some unwarranted news to promote inferior films and sell their efforts for the profit of the boss. They may have the title of publicist, or they may only get some subsidies from the boss. For example, a certain film company that specializes in shoddy manufacturing often engages in this kind of buying-up of trivial newspapers that publish film articles and trivial film critics who often write low-level interest articles. Some film critics are hired to be the editors of film publications, and some are specially invited to write film articles in some radical film journals, and some are even hired by film companies to be consultants. (Those who are consultants naturally have a more sufficient literary cultivation.)

Finally, I would like to mention the hardships of film critics. Living by writing is the most difficult kind of life, and I think writing film reviews is an even more difficult kind of life. Most of them do not have an income above maintaining life, but their cost is twice that of other writers. Film review articles are mostly "rushed" out or "forced" out. We know that each theater opens at three o'clock and closes at five o'clock. After the closing, they must set aside everything to write review articles; no matter how bad a film is, no matter whether you have any opinions on the film, you must send a thousand or several hundred words to the editor around eight o'clock. You have to watch bad films that you don't want to watch or that make people want to fall asleep; you have to write texts that you don't want to write and that are difficult to write well. There is a huge whip beating you, and you must search your brains and hand in an article. It is common to see some film critics still staring at a blank piece of paper in a long three or four hours, their writing is sluggish. Like a difficult delivery of a pregnant woman. This kind of hardship of "forcing" writing is only understood by those who have written film reviews. What is its meaning.

X X X

Special Self-Employment Introduction

A Prisoner of Life 295

— Ms. Xiangjun

Plato said: "No matter how difficult it is, never beg for pity from others, because begging for pity contains an element of contempt." Therefore, I pressed my heart into steel, enduring labor and resentment, enduring hunger and cold, struggling alone under the miserable wind and rain, and enduring all the disasters of the world. Although tears were floating in my eyes and spinning around, I swallowed them into my throat, swallowing them as the bitter juice of life, and never wept in front of cold-blooded people!

However, in this deformed society, a poor woman without a background and without a backer, exchanges bread with her own labor. Even if she is born with an iron bone, and is exploited and has her bones crushed and marrow sucked, even so, clothing and food may not necessarily be warm and full, and in the end, she cannot avoid the danger of unemployment! Ah, I really don't know what kind of human relationship-organized society this is?

It has been two years since I lost my job. I am wandering and my eyes are empty. When I think of the insults and arrogance that lonely people without social status suffer when they ask for help, it will plunge the whole soul into sadness, and the courage to survive will also decline because of this. Therefore, in this long period of unemployment, I only closed the door of the pavilion, preparing to sit and wait for death, gazing at the passing of spring and summer, and the hurried changes of the seasons, panicking like an ox trapped in a mud pit, rolling around in the mud pit, and dazed!

In the early morning, I woke up from a bitter dream, stroking the scars all over my body. The tragic life of the past was thrown into my heart more forcefully than anything else. After struggling for more than thirty years, what did I get from being cruelly tortured in the world? I can't even maintain a person's most basic life! Alas! What can human affairs be imagined? I only feel that crying and laughing are both wrong! I was like a wounded and wailing beast, collapsing and falling, and no longer had the strength to move!

At this time, I imagined the situation when the last-day writers threw themselves into the sea, such as the situation when Zhu Xiangwei Yanchi and others despaired and decided to sink. Alas! What a great temptation this is to me! In this way, I always feel that it is stronger and more tragic than begging for pity in front of cold-blooded people.

But wise readers! I have an old parent with white hair waiting for me in the corner of my hometown! Her poor old age makes me have to cheer up and be a human being for a few more days. Ah, I didn't expect her ability to be so great!

Because of this relationship, I am forced to write this article, wanting to exchange my labor for a cup of leftovers from the charitable people in society. Although I have no special skills, continuous labor is the model of my past life. For more than ten years, I have worked as a female worker in factories and teachers in family schools. Now, whatever I can do, I am willing to do, as long as there is a position. Correspondence address: c/o Mr. Chen, No. 23, Huayuanfang, Jinshenfu Road.

Amateur Study

Examples of How to Read "Literature" 296

— Xiaoshan

(1) How to read novels?

Because it is the same literary work, depending on its different forms, whether it is a novel or a drama, naturally the way to read it cannot be the same. But here we will temporarily take the novel as a representative, and let the readers deduce the special points themselves!

Mr. Yin Zuozhen, in his article on how to read novels, once proposed the following outline for reading "Wei Hu": (1) the story told in this novel; (2) the protagonist's thoughts (its transformation and development process); (3) the social basis of the protagonist's ideological transformation; (4) the author's consciousness reflected in this novel; (5) the social life form of that era expressed in this novel; (6) what are the characteristics of formal technology? Which school does it belong to? Is this formal technology consistent with its content pulse? I think this outline is more correct, and it is almost applicable to literary works of all forms, not only to reading novels. Although the second to fifth items are not conditions that are available in every work, they can always be found in each work in part or in whole, which is undoubtedly the case. The first and sixth are questions about form.

We must perform the above anatomy on a work before it can be said to be a scientific way of reading. If we only do the first step, only pay attention to the plot in the work, only have interest in the event, and do not ask about anything else, that is the so-called "lowest-level appreciation." If you focus on savoring the beauty of the work's words, tones, structure, and expression, and don't ask about anything else, that is the work of old literati who play with words. It is not a scientific method of studying literature. Both of the above methods are not enough.

Only the reader who performs the second to fifth tasks has grasped the center of the problem, which is almost the central condition of all literary works.

(2) How to perform the above reading method?

Naturally, we cannot say that the problem has been solved even if we memorize the above reading method. How do we perform this reading method?

Roughly speaking, its process is as follows:

First, browse through the selected work as quickly as possible to get a preliminary understanding of the general outline of the whole book or the whole article, and find out the main characters, the center of the story, and the development clues in the article. In this stage, it is probably enough to use your eyes.

Second, when examining the protagonist's thoughts in the story, you not only use your brain, but also your hands. You should record all the words spoken by the protagonist before and after and his personal inner thoughts, compare them with each other, and find out the route of development. This part of the work is very difficult to do. Some people read "Water Margin" and draw out the faces of the 108 heroes one by one, spending a lot of effort to compare. This is necessary, and at the same time, there cannot be any subjective likes and dislikes. If the protagonist's thoughts are contradictory before and after, if the author does not write it out for another meaning, then it can be concluded that the author's failure.

Third, in fact, this stage is carried out simultaneously with the second stage. After reading the protagonist's ideological transformation, we must further find its basis. For this, you must thoroughly understand the protagonist's social life. You should focus on the reality of society. If the protagonist's ideological transformation has no basis, then the work must be a failure. The so-called basis for ideological change is probably based on his social class, the contradictions between social groups at that time, political and economic panic, large riots, revolutions, hunger, and other phenomena.

Fourth, conduct an examination of the author's consciousness reflected in the work. This is not limited to this article. We should also find more biographies of the author, other works, and his actual living conditions to help us understand this article. This stage can be easily carried out when you have a considerable understanding of the author on weekdays.

Fifth, as for the review of the social life form of that era expressed in this work, this should have an undistorted understanding, an objective point of view, social enthusiasm, and a distance from the public, of the current international and domestic political and economic situation, the state of confrontation between social groups, and domestic and world events. This all depends on paying attention to the forms of social life at all levels on weekdays. Of course, if you do not have a little understanding of the times, you will not be able to understand the times of the work. The review of this stage is linked to the entire social periphery. It is impossible to go to society only to read a work. In this, we can also see not only how the author, but also how the reader should increase their life experience.

Sixth, regarding the technical review, this part requires readers to carefully understand it using scientific analysis methods. Originally, the so-called technology was also created by writers unconsciously. But the past experience is precious, we should accept the legacy of the previous era. The application of this stage is to read more, watch more, cut the whole article into several parts, and then form the whole from the parts, and observe from all aspects. Regarding this aspect, it is best to read more specialized books of this kind.

From the second to the sixth above, we must not only use our eyes, but also our hands, our mouths, and even our feet to visit everywhere. Therefore, reading literary books is by no means an easy task; it is by no means something that can be achieved in such a leisurely attitude as lying on a "sofa."

Amateur Sports

Sports in Prison 297

— Li Kui

Prisoners in prison also need exercise during their leisure time after work. They also know that physical exercise is as important as eating and sleeping.

However, unlike outside, where some people are chosen to stand out; there are no such things as athletes, champions, or mermaids.

They are limited by their environment, confined to small, dark cells, and have no opportunity to exercise.

But in order to prevent their health from deteriorating further, leading to illness and death, they have to exercise within a small space.

Their exercises can be roughly divided into four types:

The first type is "hitting hands." This is the most common exercise. Every time after a meal, some young prisoners gather together to "hit hands."

This "hitting hands" exercise is done like this: there must be several people participating. After joining, each person extends one hand and places it together. At the same time, another person randomly says a number. They count according to the order, and whoever counts to the last number is the first to be "hit."

The person to be "hit" must stand in front, put their left hand under their right shoulder, with the palm facing outwards, properly placed between the armpit and the back, waiting for the person standing behind to "hit." The person behind must "hit" skillfully. After the "hit," the person who was "hit" immediately turns around to guess who "hit" them. If guessed correctly, the guesser takes over the "hitting." If guessed incorrectly, the person still turns back to be "hit."

This "hitting hands" exercise not only strengthens the body but also develops judgment. It is truly one of the best exercises in prison.

The second type is "playing ball." This is not very common, and only prisoners who have lived in schools play it.

The balls they use are not the leather balls used outside. Leather balls are not allowed inside. The balls they use are made of rice.

Every day at mealtime, those who love to play ball always secretly save a handful of rice. Even if there is very little rice, they would rather eat one less bite themselves and still save a handful.

They slowly rub the saved rice finely with their hands, like smooth noodles. Afterwards, they knead it into round rice balls. After letting them dry for a while, when thrown against the wall, they become very bouncy and can bounce back immediately like a rubber ball.

This way, they can have a competition. Whoever participates comes up to "hit" in order, like playing tennis. Whoever "games" immediately comes down, and the second person continues to "hit."

This "playing ball" exercise is also a good exercise for prisoners. However, sometimes problems arise. If the rice ball is seen by the warden, they will be scolded, and that's not all. The rice ration will also be reduced immediately. The reason is wasting rice!

The third type is running. In winter, when it is unbearably cold and there is no way to get warm in the tattered bedding, they have to "dance" in the cell at night -- actually, they are not dancing. They have never danced before, and they have never even been to those grand dance halls. They are just jumping around to keep warm, a euphemism. During the day, they run in the alley. Whenever they start running, almost all the prisoners in the entire alley participate, except for a few old men with weak legs standing in the doorway watching.

One after another, they run back and forth in that alley, which is about twenty steps long and two or three feet wide. They don't rest until they are sweating.

This exercise is sometimes interfered with because the sound of running footsteps is too loud. The military police will run to the entrance of the alley and roar angrily while knocking on the iron gate.

The fourth type is swimming. This exercise also borrows a term. There is no swimming pool in prison, so how can they swim? Isn't this borrowing a term?

This is when they are unbearably hot, they use wooden basins to hold water and splash each other in the alley, making a noisy commotion, which is like swimming.

This exercise is just a disguised bath. This exercise is even more often subject to interference. But because they are unbearably hot, they know they will be scolded or even beaten, but they still splash each other as before.

These few exercises in prison are very pitiful! If you compare them with exercises outside, there is a world of difference!

Being limited by their environment, they can do this much, which is very satisfying. Moreover, these exercises are universal. Their exercises are for everyone's health, not just for a few people to show off.

Science Miscellany

The Story of the Invention of the Airship (9) 300

— Shu Lin

The successful Zeppelin of 1905 had a volume of 11,300 cubic meters, which was unprecedentedly large. It was 128 meters long, 11 meters in diameter at its widest point, equipped with two 85-horsepower engines, and had a speed of 11 meters per second.

People who previously had antipathy towards Zeppelin all reversed their previous attitude and became admirers.

Later, the Zeppelin Airship Company was established, manufacturing airships in large quantities. From 1900 to 1924, a total of 129 ships were built. Among them, 48 belonged to the army, 65 belonged to the navy, and the rest were used for non-military purposes.

Everyone knows that Zeppelin airships established great achievements for Germany during the European War. However, the world knows very little about Zeppelin's arduous struggles. Seven of the airships Zeppelin built himself were destroyed by storms and fires. However, each failure encouraged Zeppelin with new energy, like a tumbler, repeatedly falling and rising. When we understand the career of this gray-haired old man, how will it stimulate our new feelings?

In 1913, when Zeppelin celebrated his 75th birthday, all of Germany celebrated together, and a grand celebration was held in Friedrichshafen. At that time, the German Emperor sent the following congratulatory message to Zeppelin:

"The existence of the brave and great man who conquered the sky is the honor of the German Empire!"

Indeed, not only the German Emperor, but all the German people were proud of Zeppelin. The value and structure of Zeppelin-type airships are set aside for the moment; his life itself is already a representative of the German soul.

5. Zeppelin-type Airship's Night Raid on London

Finally, let us talk about the story of the Zeppelin-type airship's night raid on London.

German Air Force Commander Colonel Moltke made the following remarks about the night raid on London. Colonel Moltke himself was a person who personally experienced the night raid on London by airship.

"The citizens of London are afraid of our Zeppelin's attack. They do not light a lamp at night and prohibit the use of matches on the streets. However, we do not find this difficult. The airship came to the sky above London, which happened to be a starry and moonlit night. There was no fog on the streets of London, and a layer of hazy curtain enveloped it. Under this curtain, the entire London slept quietly, and my heart beat strangely hard. The Thames River reflected the twilight of the sky, reflecting a silver-gray light. We dropped the bombs we brought. Parking lots and bridges were the most targeted by our snipers, and at the same time, we prayed that we would not hurt non-combatant women and children (note: this statement is completely contradictory)." (To be continued)

Shen Bao This City Supplement Movie Special

Hollywood's Star School 301

— Mi Qi

Many Talents Emerge from its Doors and Walls; the School Declares This is Not a Shortcut to Success

This school is not called the Hollywood Star School, but because it is located in Hollywood, the world's film capital, and many of its graduates are famous in the film industry, everyone calls that school the School of Stars. In fact, its name is Hollywood High School. Now I will talk about some things about this school.

There are no less than tens of millions of primary and secondary schools in the United States. Among them, there are no less than millions of school-age children who are thinking about entering the film industry in the future. Every year, countless children, both male and female, from far and near, run to Hollywood, wanting to try their skills. Almost all of them are abandoning school and leaving their families at the age of middle school to come to the film capital to seek opportunities. They often wait for an opportunity without eating for several days. They are poor and in distress, and they are willing to do anything... washing dishes, taking care of children, working as waiters in restaurants... etc.... hoping that one day they will enter the film industry. They are not afraid of disappointment. They think that if they persevere, one day there will be a miracle that falls on their heads. But in the end, the god of opportunity does not often descend, and the result obtained by most young men and women is heartbreak, disillusionment, hunger, and wandering. But they continue to come and continue to hope. "How many of these school-age young men and women have the hope of succeeding in the film industry? Is it wise for them to abandon their studies and come to seek the source of gold? Should they graduate from local schools in their hometowns first? If you ask the graduates of Hollywood High School this question, they will tell you that you should continue your studies. You don't have to wait in front of the film companies every day. You should put some effort into your books! Because they are in a close position, they understand everything in the film city more clearly. They will advise you not to leave your studies and family and come to this place where there are too many people and no place to set foot!

Strangely enough, many graduates of this Hollywood High School have entered the film industry and succeeded. One graduate said: "When I was studying there, Faye, Marceline Day, and Clayton Chaney were in the same history class as me; William Keenan was in the same English class as me; Marilyn Burns and Irene Murray were members of our literary society; Marilyn Marsh left school to film with John Barrymore; among the classmates, those who are now famous in the film industry also include Bodil Rosing, Barbara Kent, Ben Alexander, Alice White, etc., seven or eight people. But among them, with two exceptions, none of them thought about entering the film industry when they were in school. Not only do the students not pay attention to film affairs, but also the school authorities are most unhappy to hear people say: 'That school is a training center for stars.' There is an English teacher named William Dooper. Of the ten famous film figures who graduated from there, nine came from under his tutelage. But he said: 'We try our best to prevent students who are determined to pursue a career in film from enrolling. Our school is one of the most advanced secondary schools in the country. Therefore, we should maintain the reputation and status of our school, and not truly reduce it to a recruitment agency for film companies. If students want to take this place as a place to rest and wait quietly for opportunities in the film industry, rather than truly come here to study, we will not recognize them as our good students and must exclude them!'"

As for the students, they also occasionally work as extras in film companies to earn some pocket money. But this does not violate the school's regulations, and it is common throughout the United States to find small jobs to earn money to maintain personal livelihood. Hollywood cannot be regarded as an exception. However, the students unanimously agree with the school authorities' policy of maintaining the dignity of the school. They say that although many graduates of the school have succeeded in the film industry, this does not affect the school's studies, academic style, etc. Moreover, in fact, the path for male and female students graduating from Hollywood High School to enter the film industry is not more convenient than those from other schools.

Film Review

Review of "Love's Magic" 302

— Ling He

Sisters Under The Skin

丨Cathay丨

Indeed, Columbia Pictures has recently been "making great strides." From "Madame" and "It Happened One Night" to this "Love's Magic," the producers have indeed abandoned those Western film plans and are producing so-called big films on a large scale. This has somewhat changed the audience's previous bad impressions of the company. However, this does not mean that "Madame" or "It Happened One Night" are completely successful works, but rather that the bad habit of shoddy production is now almost completely eliminated.

As far as this "Love's Magic" is concerned, we feel that the director's technique is the first thing worth noting. I may not be very familiar with the name David Burton, but in terms of his achievements in this film, there are many things that deserve our praise.

First, the Montage is very compact and concise. There are no trivial scenes in it, and every scene is necessary for the drama. For example, the various pleasures enjoyed by the male and female protagonists in London and Paris, as well as the various scenes of the female protagonist in jewelry stores and hat shops, are all high-speed reproductions. In addition, many unnecessary processes are very cleanly omitted.

Second, what we should pay attention to is the Tempo's speed. This is naturally inextricably linked to the Montage, and can also be said to belong to the Montage. The reason why it should be particularly pointed out is that the high-speed development of the aforementioned scenes, in depicting the need to emphasize the stimulation of noble people in decadent enjoyment, this high-speed fast is indeed the best expression method. And when Ye Si returned to his office disheartened, and when he discovered the inner pain of his lover before, that extremely slow tone, for the help of the protagonist's inner heart, in the extremely quiet air, is really very effective.

Third, the director's meticulous attention to the development of each scene is also worth noting. When the male and female protagonists first meet in the garden, the man kisses her forcefully, and the woman refuses and slaps him in the face. (This is a foreshadowing for later.) When Ye Si learned the true attitude of his lover towards himself, before he came to her house and entered the room, he approached the mirror, looked at his old face, and saw a pot of delicate flowers on the table. Immediately, he felt cold, tightened his clothes, and walked into the room sadly and calmly. . . . . . From these places, we can feel a kind of cold emotion, and this is obtained through delicate scenes.

Fourth, what we can talk about is the vibrancy of the shots. As mentioned earlier, the complex scenes of enjoyment, shopping, and buying clothes, those many low-angle shots are really very commendable. However, his angle of the shots is not lively for no reason. For example, when the male and female protagonists climbed the stairs step by step with the musician, in order to show the youth and old age between them, the camera has always been shooting from above. The two young people walked quickly and effortlessly, while Ye Si was very labored and finally sat on the stairs to rest, panting. Until the female protagonist came back to support him, the camera remained at the same angle. But we don't feel bored because in this way, the contrast between their vigor and twilight is very clear and moving. As for when the musician is playing a sad violin, taking close-ups of each face with the same emotion under different angles, and then Dissolving to the stage and the surrounding audience, are all worth learning from.

Fifth, as for other descriptions of the surrounding air, such as using rain to write about the depression of the mood, using the summer night's moon and wind to write about the male protagonist's leisurely mood, and using the breeze of the window curtains to write about the warmth of the hidden boudoir, from these places, the director quite used symbolic techniques and achieved good results.

As mentioned above, naturally we cannot ignore that most of this is the success of the script. This is not only because the playwright fully paid attention to the use of film art in the creative process, but also because we cannot deny that it has a certain degree of seriousness in the theme. Of course, what is written here is only limited to the scope of love, and it is indeed not easy to write about a 50-year-old person who wants to obtain true love. In the end, it is a terrible disillusionment. From this aspect, the intermediate process is indeed quite realistically written and very attractive. This is also the playwright's ultimate goal. But due to the choice of subject matter, what kind of impression does it give us in terms of the effect of the drama? That Ye Si devoted his life to making money and could not get the opportunity to enjoy himself. Although he had a kind heart, he bought the love of a young girl with a lot of money, but in the end, due to age, he only limited the girl to the pain of love. A lot of money, after all, cannot buy back the lost youth. In the end, he was disheartened and, after being hurt once, returned to his career. This, that wealthy Ye Si, made the audience very sympathetic.

In American films, it is always difficult to leave this aspect of preaching, but because of its weight, it does not make us very disgusted. However, in objectively appreciating a work of art, perhaps we should pay more attention to their expression methods. At least, like many successful old-fashioned literary works, there are many things that are worth our criticism and appreciation.

The heroine Elizabeth Allan writes well, but there is nothing outstanding, and the success of the male lead Frank Morgan in this film is something we should be surprised about. The other two supporting roles – Ye Si's wife and the musician – are both competent.

Luo Mingyou Returns to the Country and Arrives in Hong Kong 303

Luo Mingyou, the general manager of Lianhua, was dispatched by the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministry of Industry as a commissioner to investigate the European and American film industry and the film industry. He took the President Hoover to go abroad on April 24th of this year. Mr. Luo traveled to famous factories in Europe and the United States. He conducted a very detailed investigation of the conditions of the film industry in various countries, the equipment of film production, the creation of technology, the lives and service spirit of film practitioners. This work has benefited him a lot. Now, Mr. Luo has completed his investigation and returned to the country and arrived in Hong Kong. After arriving in Hong Kong, he still needs a short period of rest and sorting out of the report before he can come to Shanghai and turn to Beijing to report.

"Hometown" is Produced with Dubbing 304

Shen Xiling has been silent for a long time since "Twenty-Four Hours in Shanghai." Recently, "Hometown," which he wrote himself, has passed and started work. In terms of actors, Xuan Jinglin plays a crazy old woman, Gao Qianping plays a wandering girl, Sun Min plays a lecherous young man, Zhao Dan plays a lame old man, and Mei Xi plays a revolutionary youth. It can be said that they are all very competent. Because Shen Xiling himself and the Mingxing Company attach great importance to this play, they decided to produce it with dubbing.

Time flies so fast. The film "Song of the Fishermen." From the premiere to now. Counting on my fingers. It has been more than fifty days without realizing it. From today onwards, the theater will give away a photo of Ruan Lingyu in the film "New Woman" as a thank you to the audience. It is extremely precious and beautiful. Watching a good film and getting a valuable photo. This is indeed a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity.

Film Novel

Wonderful Son, Wonderful Wife (Born to Be Kissed) (14) 306

— Translated by Yours Truly

After the photographer shouted loudly, the bedroom door of Pan Qi's ship suddenly opened, and a person jumped out. It was a beautiful woman, wearing only a white dress as thin as cicada wings, with her flesh color vaguely visible. The beautiful woman jumped straight out of the room, as if there were tigers eating her inside, rushing to Pan Qi's side, hugging him tightly, burying her head directly in his arms, and shouting loudly, "Daddy!" At this moment, the camera clicked, and the true scene was captured in the lens. Pan Qi frantically shouted, "Slow down!" But the photographer had already been squeezed into the crowd, and his whereabouts were unknown. And Yi Di also retreated to the bedroom like a startled swan, slamming the door shut. At this time, the news reporters believed that this was the best possible news, and immediately surrounded him, asking, "Mr. Pan Qi, do you have anything to announce?"

At this time, Yi Di had already run to the house of Que Li · Tongna. Jidi was arguing with her, telling her to go back, but Yi Di refused, determined not to talk about love anymore, and to be a good woman. She told Jidi to go home alone. Jidi wanted to pull her away, but Yi Di pushed her away like a madwoman. Jidi had no choice but to walk out of Tongna's door alone. As soon as Jidi stepped down the stairs, a person came running towards her and bumped into her. Jidi was startled when she saw it was Tom. Tom asked, "Where is Yi Di?" Jidi said, "Upstairs!" Tom pushed Jidi aside! and also pushed away the doorman of Tongna's house, and ran straight upstairs. Jidi chased desperately from behind. As soon as he went upstairs, he ran to the room where Tongna and Yi Di were standing. Without saying a word, he punched Tongna in the face. Then, without saying a word, he pulled Yi Di to the bathroom, turned on the cold water tap to the maximum, and dunked her head in the cold water. Yi Di struggled fiercely, but Tom was incredibly strong, and she couldn't break free. Tom then said resentfully, "You're drunk. I'm here to save you, even if it means drowning you!" Yi Di managed to catch her breath and shouted, "Tom, it's too late!" Tom's hand loosened when he heard this, and his face turned white. He quickly asked, "Too late? Have you and Tongna already..." Yi Di said, "No. Your father has already fallen for one of my tricks!" She wanted to tell Tom about what had happened in the past. But she saw a person standing outside the door, it was Pan Qi himself, so she stopped talking. Pan Qi said angrily, "You really know how to trick me!" Yi Di teased him, "Okay, Mr. Ambassador, think twice before you try to trap a woman again!" Pan Qi pulled Yi Di and Tom out together, where Tongna was still touching his cheek, which was throbbing with pain. Pan Qi shouted at Yi Di, "Be careful, I'm not finished with you yet!" Yi Di also retorted without showing any weakness, "You be careful too! If you do anything to me again, I'll tell the news reporters!" Pan Qi said, "Even if you tell the news reporters, you have to say it my way!" Yi Di said, "What's your way of saying it?" Pan Qi said, "I've already told them that you're a good person. This matter was entirely fabricated by my political enemies. As for why you're in my house? It's because you're my daughter-in-law..." He turned to look at Tom and said, "Your wife!" He then grabbed Yi Di's hand again and said, "It's getting late. The shipowner can't wait for us to board all night!" Tom wrung his hands and said, "If only we could get a marriage license!" Pan Qi said, "You don't need to worry about anything, I've taken care of everything for you." He opened the door to the living room, and a pastor and others were standing outside. Pan Qi also pulled the shocked Jidi and the still-aching Tongna to be witnesses. Yi Di even smiled at Pan Qi and said, "Don't tell me this is another one of your tricks, trying to escape a difficult situation?" Pan Qi laughed, "Don't worry. I've struggled my whole life to get here. Now that I have you, the family will have descendants!" (The End)
